#### Abstracts
##### **When RAG Chatbots Expose Their Backend: An Anonymized Case Study of Privacy and Security Risks in Patient-Facing Medical AI**
2605.00796v1 by Alfredo Madrid-García, Miguel Rujas

Background: Patient-facing medical chatbots based on retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) are increasingly promoted to deliver accessible, grounded health information. AI-assisted development lowers the barrier to building them, but they still demand rigorous security, privacy, and governance controls. Objective: To report an anonymized, non-destructive security assessment of a publicly accessible patient-facing medical RAG chatbot and identify governance lessons for safe deployment of generative AI in health. Methods: We used a two-stage strategy. First, Claude Opus 4.6 supported exploratory prompt-based testing and structured vulnerability hypotheses. Second, candidate findings were manually verified using Chrome Developer Tools, inspecting browser-visible network traffic, payloads, API schemas, configuration objects, and stored interaction data. Results: The LLM-assisted phase identified a critical vulnerability: sensitive system and RAG configuration appeared exposed through client-server communication rather than restricted server-side. Manual verification confirmed that ordinary browser inspection allowed collection of the system prompt, model and embedding configuration, retrieval parameters, backend endpoints, API schema, document and chunk metadata, knowledge-base content, and the 1,000 most recent patient-chatbot conversations. The deployment also contradicted its privacy assurances: full conversation records, including health-related queries, were retrievable without authentication. Conclusions: Serious privacy and security failures in patient-facing RAG chatbots can be identified with standard browser tools, without specialist skills or authentication; independent review should be a prerequisite for deployment. Commercial LLMs accelerated this assessment, including under a false developer persona; assistance available to auditors is equally available to adversaries.

摘要：背景：基於檢索增強生成（RAG）的面向患者的醫療聊天機器人越來越受到推廣，以提供可獲得的、基於事實的健康資訊。AI輔助的開發降低了構建它們的門檻，但仍然需要嚴格的安全性、隱私和治理控制。<lb/>目標：報告一個公開可訪問的面向患者的醫療RAG聊天機器人的匿名、非破壞性安全評估，並確定安全部署生成性AI於健康領域的治理教訓。<lb/>方法：我們使用了兩階段策略。首先，Claude Opus 4.6支持探索性基於提示的測試和結構化的漏洞假設。<lb/>其次，使用Chrome開發者工具手動驗證候選發現，檢查瀏覽器可見的網絡流量、有效載荷、API架構、配置對象和存儲的交互數據。<lb/>結果：LLM輔助階段識別了一個關鍵漏洞：敏感系統和RAG配置似乎通過客戶端-服務器通信暴露，而不是限制在服務器端。<lb/>手動驗證確認，普通的瀏覽器檢查允許收集系統提示、模型和嵌入配置、檢索參數、後端端點、API架構、文檔和片段元數據、知識庫內容，以及最近1,000個患者-聊天機器人對話的記錄。<lb/>該部署還違背了其隱私保證：包括健康相關查詢的完整對話記錄可以在未經身份驗證的情況下檢索。<lb/>結論：面向患者的RAG聊天機器人中嚴重的隱私和安全失敗可以通過標準瀏覽器工具識別，而無需專業技能或身份驗證；獨立審查應該是部署的前提。<lb/>商業LLM加速了這一評估，包括在虛假開發者身份下；可用於審計員的協助同樣可用於對手。

##### **To Call or Not to Call: A Framework to Assess and Optimize LLM Tool Calling**
2605.00737v1 by Qinyuan Wu, Soumi Das, Mahsa Amani, Arijit Nag, Seungeon Lee, Krishna P. Gummadi, Abhilasha Ravichander, Muhammad Bilal Zafar

Agentic AI architectures augment LLMs with external tools, unlocking strong capabilities. However, tool use is not always beneficial; some calls may be redundant or even harmful. Effective tool use, therefore, hinges on a core LLM decision: whether to call or not call a tool, when performing a task. This decision is particularly challenging for web search tools, where the benefits of external information depend on the model's internal knowledge and its ability to integrate potentially noisy tool responses. We introduce a principled framework inspired by decision-making theory to evaluate web search tool-use decisions along three key factors: necessity, utility, and affordability. Our analysis combines two complementary lenses: a normative perspective that infers true need and utility from an optimal allocation of tool calls, and a descriptive perspective that infers the model's self-perceived need and utility from their observed behaviors. We find that models' perceived need and utility of tool calls are often misaligned with their true need and utility. Building on this framework, we train lightweight estimators of need and utility based on models' hidden states. Our estimators enable simple controllers that can improve decision quality and lead to stronger task performance than the self-perceived set up across three tasks and six models.

摘要：代理 AI 架構透過外部工具增強 LLM 的能力，解鎖強大的功能。<lb/>然而，工具的使用並不總是有益的；某些呼叫可能是多餘的，甚至有害。<lb/>因此，有效的工具使用取決於一個核心 LLM 決策：在執行任務時，是否呼叫工具。<lb/>這一決策對於網路搜索工具尤其具有挑戰性，因為外部資訊的好處依賴於模型的內部知識及其整合潛在嘈雜工具回應的能力。<lb/>我們引入了一個受決策理論啟發的原則框架，以評估網路搜索工具使用決策，並考量三個關鍵因素：必要性、效用和可負擔性。<lb/>我們的分析結合了兩個互補的視角：一個規範性視角，從最佳的工具呼叫分配推斷真正的需求和效用；另一個描述性視角，從觀察到的行為推斷模型自我感知的需求和效用。<lb/>我們發現模型對工具呼叫的自我感知需求和效用往往與其真正的需求和效用不一致。<lb/>基於這一框架，我們訓練了基於模型隱藏狀態的輕量級需求和效用估算器。<lb/>我們的估算器使簡單的控制器能夠提高決策質量，並在三個任務和六個模型中帶來比自我感知設置更強的任務表現。

##### **EASE: Federated Multimodal Unlearning via Entanglement-Aware Anchor Closure**
2605.00733v1 by Zihao Ding, Beining Wu, Jun Huang

Federated Multimodal Learning (FML) trains multimodal models across decentralized clients while keeping their image-text pairs private. However, joint embedding training entangles forgotten knowledge across both modalities and client gradient subspaces, hindering federated unlearning. Previous federated unlearning approaches neither sever the cross-modal reconstruction channel mediated by bilinear coupling nor separate forget-exclusive update directions from those shared with retained clients. We identify an Anchor Principle for federated multimodal contrastive unlearning: forgotten alignments persist through three residual anchors arising from bilinear cross-modal coupling, principal-angle subspace entanglement, and continued federated updates. At the modality level, we show that bilateral displacement of both visual and language branches closes the cross-modal reconstruction channel. Correspondingly, our method addresses subspace entanglement through Cosine--Sine decomposition of client-update subspaces, isolating forget-exclusive directions from retain support. Moreover, we propose a direction-selective Forget Lock that bounds residual drift across rounds. Combining these strategies, we present EASE, an Entanglement-Aware Subspace Excision framework that closes all three anchor channels under a unified design. EASE demonstrates consistent superiority across multiple datasets and unlearning scenarios, for instance, matching the retrain reference to within 0.2 and 4.2 R@1 points on the forget and retain sides under client unlearning on Flickr30K with CLIP-B/32.

摘要：聯邦多模態學習（FML）在去中心化的客戶端之間訓練多模態模型，同時保持其圖像-文本對的私密性。<lb/>然而，聯合嵌入訓練在兩種模態和客戶端梯度子空間之間糾纏了被遺忘的知識，妨礙了聯邦遺忘。<lb/>先前的聯邦遺忘方法既未切斷由雙線性耦合介導的跨模態重建通道，也未將遺忘專屬的更新方向與保留客戶共享的方向分開。<lb/>我們確定了一個聯邦多模態對比遺忘的錨原則：被遺忘的對齊通過三個來自雙線性跨模態耦合、主角子空間糾纏和持續的聯邦更新的殘餘錨持續存在。<lb/>在模態層面上，我們展示了視覺和語言分支的雙邊位移關閉了跨模態重建通道。<lb/>相應地，我們的方法通過客戶端更新子空間的餘弦-正弦分解來解決子空間糾纏，將遺忘專屬的方向與保留支持隔離開。<lb/>此外，我們提出了一個方向選擇性遺忘鎖，限制了跨輪次的殘餘漂移。<lb/>結合這些策略，我們提出了EASE，一個考慮糾纏的子空間切除框架，在統一設計下關閉所有三個錨通道。<lb/>EASE在多個數據集和遺忘場景中顯示出一致的優越性，例如，在Flickr30K上進行客戶端遺忘時，將重訓參考匹配至遺忘和保留側的0.2和4.2 R@1點內，使用CLIP-B/32。

##### **Empowering Heterogeneous Graph Foundation Models via Decoupled Relation Alignment**
2605.00731v1 by Ziyu Zheng, Yaming Yang, Zhe Wang, Ziyu Guan, Wei Zhao

While Graph Foundation Models (GFMs) have achieved remarkable success in homogeneous graphs, extending them to multi-domain heterogeneous graphs (MDHGs) remains a formidable challenge due to cross-type feature shifts and intra-domain relation gaps. Existing global feature alignment methods (PCA or SVD) enforce a shared feature space blindly, which distorts type-specific semantics and disrupts original topologies, inevitably leading to "Type Collapse" and "Relation Confusion". To address these fundamental limitations, we propose Decoupled relation Subspace Alignment (DRSA), a novel, plug-and-play relation-driven alignment framework. DRSA fundamentally shifts the paradigm by decoupling feature semantics from relation structures. Specifically, it introduces a dual-relation subspace projection mechanism to coordinate cross-type interactions within a shared low-rank relation subspace explicitly. Furthermore, a feature-structure decoupled representation is designed to decompose aligned features into a semantic projection component and a structural residual term, adaptively absorbing intra-domain variations. Optimized via a stable alternating minimization strategy based on Block Coordinate Descent, DRSA constructs a well-calibrated, structure-aware latent space. Extensive experiments on multiple real-world benchmark datasets demonstrate that DRSA can be seamlessly integrated as a universal preprocessing module, significantly and consistently enhancing the cross-domain and few-shot knowledge transfer capabilities of state-of-the-art GFMs. The code is available at: https://github.com/zhengziyu77/DSRA.

摘要：雖然圖形基礎模型（GFMs）在同質圖中取得了顯著成功，但將其擴展到多領域異質圖（MDHGs）仍然是一個艱巨的挑戰，因為存在跨類型特徵轉移和域內關係差距。現有的全球特徵對齊方法（PCA或SVD）盲目強制共享特徵空間，這會扭曲類型特定的語義並破壞原始拓撲，必然導致“類型崩潰”和“關係混淆”。為了解決這些基本限制，我們提出了解耦關係子空間對齊（DRSA），這是一種新穎的即插即用關係驅動對齊框架。DRSA 從根本上改變了範式，通過將特徵語義與關係結構解耦。具體而言，它引入了一種雙關係子空間投影機制，以明確協調共享低秩關係子空間中的跨類型交互。此外，設計了一種特徵-結構解耦表示，以將對齊特徵分解為語義投影組件和結構殘差項，自適應地吸收域內變化。通過基於區塊坐標下降的穩定交替最小化策略進行優化，DRSA 構建了一個良好校準的結構感知潛在空間。在多個現實世界基準數據集上的廣泛實驗表明，DRSA 可以無縫集成作為通用預處理模塊，顯著且持續地增強最先進的 GFMs 的跨域和少樣本知識轉移能力。代碼可在以下網址獲得：https://github.com/zhengziyu77/DSRA。

##### **SC-Taxo: Hierarchical Taxonomy Generation under Semantic Consistency Constraints using Large Language Models**
2605.00620v1 by Shiqiang Cai, Nianhong Niu, Shizhu He, Kang Liu, Jun Zhao

Scientific literature is expanding at an unprecedented pace, making it increasingly challenging to efficiently organize and access domain knowledge. A high-quality scientific taxonomy offers a structured and hierarchical representation of a research field, facilitating literature exploration and topic navigation, as well as enabling downstream applications such as trend analysis, idea generation, and information retrieval. However, existing taxonomy generation approaches often suffer from structural inconsistencies and semantic misalignment across hierarchical levels. Through empirical analysis, we find that these issues largely stem from inadequate modeling of hierarchical semantic consistency. To address this limitation, we propose a semantic-consistent taxonomy generation (SC-Taxo) framework that leverages large language models (LLMs) with hierarchy-aware refinement stages to ensure semantic consistency. Specifically, SC-Taxo introduces a bidirectional heading generation mechanism that jointly performs bottom-up abstraction and top-down semantic constraint, while further capturing peer-level semantic dependencies to enhance horizontal consistency. Experiments on multiple benchmark datasets demonstrate consistent improvements in hierarchy alignment and heading quality, and additional evaluation on Chinese scientific literature validates its robust cross-lingual generalization.

摘要：科學文獻以空前的速度擴展，使得有效組織和訪問領域知識變得越來越具挑戰性。高品質的科學分類法提供了研究領域的結構化和分層表示，促進文獻探索和主題導航，並使得下游應用如趨勢分析、創意生成和信息檢索成為可能。然而，現有的分類法生成方法往往存在結構不一致和層級間語義不對齊的問題。通過實證分析，我們發現這些問題主要源於對層級語義一致性建模的不充分。為了解決這一限制，我們提出了一個語義一致的分類法生成（SC-Taxo）框架，該框架利用大型語言模型（LLMs）並結合層級感知的精煉階段，以確保語義一致性。具體而言，SC-Taxo 引入了一種雙向標題生成機制，該機制同時執行自下而上的抽象和自上而下的語義約束，同時進一步捕捉同級語義依賴，以增強橫向一致性。在多個基準數據集上的實驗顯示了層級對齊和標題質量的一致性改善，並對中國科學文獻的額外評估驗證了其強大的跨語言泛化能力。

##### **Hierarchical Abstract Tree for Cross-Document Retrieval-Augmented Generation**
2605.00529v1 by Ziwen Zhao, Menglin Yang

Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) enhances large language models with external knowledge, and tree-based RAG organizes documents into hierarchical indexes to support queries at multiple granularities. However, existing Tree-RAG methods designed for single-document retrieval face critical challenges in scaling to cross-document multi-hop questions: (1) poor distribution adaptability, where $k$-means clustering introduces noise due to rigid distribution assumptions; (2) structural isolation, as tree indexes lack explicit cross-document connections; and (3) coarse abstraction, which obscures fine-grained details. To address these limitations, we propose $Ψ$-RAG, a tree-RAG framework with two key components. First, a hierarchical abstract tree index built through an iterative "merging and collapse" process that adapts to data distributions without a priori assumption. Second, a multi-granular retrieval agent that intelligently interacts with the knowledge base with reorganized queries and an agent-powered hybrid retriever. $Ψ$-RAG supports diverse tasks from token-level question answering to document-level summarization. On cross-document multi-hop QA benchmarks, it outperforms RAPTOR by 25.9% and HippoRAG 2 by 7.4% in average F1 score. Code is available at https://github.com/Newiz430/Psi-RAG.

摘要：檢索增強生成（RAG）透過外部知識增強大型語言模型，而基於樹的 RAG 將文檔組織成層次索引，以支持多層次的查詢。<lb/>然而，現有的單文檔檢索設計的 Tree-RAG 方法在擴展到跨文檔的多跳問題時面臨重大挑戰：（1）分佈適應性差，因為 $k$-均值聚類由於僵化的分佈假設而引入噪聲；<lb/>（2）結構孤立，因為樹索引缺乏明確的跨文檔連接；<lb/>（3）粗略抽象，模糊了細微的細節。<lb/>為了解決這些限制，我們提出了 $Ψ$-RAG，一個具有兩個關鍵組件的樹-RAG 框架。<lb/>首先，通過迭代的“合併與崩潰”過程構建的層次抽象樹索引，能夠根據數據分佈進行調整，而不需要事先假設。<lb/>其次，一個多層次檢索代理，能夠智能地與知識庫互動，通過重新組織的查詢和代理驅動的混合檢索器。<lb/>$Ψ$-RAG 支持從標記級問題回答到文檔級摘要的多樣任務。<lb/>在跨文檔多跳 QA 基準上，它的平均 F1 分數比 RAPTOR 高出 25.9%，比 HippoRAG 2 高出 7.4%。<lb/>代碼可在 https://github.com/Newiz430/Psi-RAG 獲得。

##### **ControBench: An Interaction-Aware Benchmark for Controversial Discourse Analysis on Social Networks**
2605.00513v1 by Ta Thanh Thuy, Jiaqi Zhu, Xuan Liu, Lin Shang, Reihaneh Rabbany, Guillaume Rabusseau, Lihui Chen, Zheng Yilun, Sitao Luan

Understanding how people argue across ideological divides online is important for studying political polarization, misinformation, and content moderation. Existing datasets capture only part of this problem: some preserve text but ignore interaction structure, some model structure without rich semantics, and others represent conversations without stable user-level ideological identity. We introduce ControBench, a benchmark for controversial discourse analysis that combines heterogeneous social interaction graphs with rich textual semantics. Built from Reddit discussions on three topics, Trump, abortion, and religion, ControBench contains 7,370 users, 1,783 posts, and 26,525 interactions. The graph contains user and post nodes connected by semantically enriched edges; in particular, user-comment-user edges encode both a reply and the parent comment that it responds to, preserving local argumentative context. User labels are derived from self-declared Reddit flairs, providing a scalable proxy for ideological identity without manual annotation. The resulting datasets exhibit low or negative adjusted homophily (Trump: -0.77, Abortion: 0.06, Religion: 0.04), reflecting the cross-cutting structure of real-world debate. We evaluate graph neural networks, pretrained language models, and large language models on ControBench and observe distinct performance patterns across topics and model families, especially when ideological boundaries are ambiguous. These results position ControBench as a challenging and realistic benchmark for controversial discourse analysis.

摘要：理解人們如何在意識形態的分歧中進行線上辯論，對於研究政治極化、錯誤資訊和內容管理至關重要。現有的數據集僅捕捉到這一問題的一部分：有些保留了文本但忽略了互動結構，有些則模擬結構卻缺乏豐富的語義，而其他則在沒有穩定用戶層面意識形態身份的情況下表示對話。我們介紹了ControBench，一個結合異質社交互動圖和豐富文本語義的爭議性話語分析基準。ControBench基於三個主題的Reddit討論構建，即特朗普、墮胎和宗教，包含7,370名用戶、1,783條帖子和26,525次互動。該圖包含用戶和帖子節點，通過語義豐富的邊連接；特別是，用戶-評論-用戶邊編碼了回覆及其所回覆的父評論，保留了局部的辯論上下文。用戶標籤來自自我聲明的Reddit標籤，提供了一種可擴展的意識形態身份代理，無需手動註釋。結果數據集顯示出低或負的調整同質性（特朗普：-0.77，墮胎：0.06，宗教：0.04），反映了現實世界辯論的交叉結構。我們在ControBench上評估圖神經網絡、預訓練語言模型和大型語言模型，並觀察到不同主題和模型家族之間的明顯性能模式，特別是在意識形態邊界模糊的情況下。這些結果使ControBench成為一個具有挑戰性和現實性的爭議性話語分析基準。

##### **Scalable Context-Aware Graph Attention for Unsupervised Anomaly Detection in Large-Scale Mobile Networks**
2605.00482v1 by Sara Malacarne, Eirik Hoel-Høiseth, Erlend Aune, David Zsolt Biró, Massimiliano Ruocco

Mobile network operators must monitor thousands of heterogeneous network elements across the radio access network and the packet core, each exposing high-dimensional KPI time series. The scale and cost of incident labelling make supervised approaches impractical, motivating unsupervised anomaly detection robust to context shifts and nonstationarity.
  We propose \textbf{C-MTAD-GAT} (\emph{Context-aware Multivariate Time-series Anomaly Detection with Graph Attention}), an anomaly detection framework designed to operate as a single shared model across large populations of network elements. The model combines temporal and feature-wise graph attention with lightweight static and dynamic context conditioning and a dual-head decoder for reconstruction and multi-step forecasting. It produces per-element, per-feature anomaly scores, converted to alerts via fully unsupervised thresholds calibrated from validation residuals.
  On the TELCO dataset released with DC-VAE \cite{garcia2023onemodel}, C-MTAD-GAT improves event-level affiliation and pointwise F1 while generating fewer alarms than prior graph-attention and VAE-based baselines. We then apply the same system to nation-scale radio access and evolved packet core control-plane counter data from a mobile network operator, where it is deployed. Operator feedback indicates the alerts are actionable and support daily monitoring, showing scalability across domains without relying on labelled incidents.

摘要：行動網路運營商必須監控無數異質的網路元素，這些元素遍佈於無線接入網路和封包核心中，每個元素都顯示出高維的KPI時間序列。事件標記的規模和成本使得監督式方法變得不切實際，這促使我們尋求對上下文變化和非平穩性具有魯棒性的無監督異常檢測。<lb/>  
我們提出了\textbf{C-MTAD-GAT}（\emph{具上下文感知的多變量時間序列異常檢測與圖注意力}），這是一個設計為在大量網路元素中作為單一共享模型運作的異常檢測框架。該模型結合了時間和特徵圖注意力，並使用輕量級的靜態和動態上下文條件，以及雙頭解碼器進行重建和多步預測。它生成每個元素、每個特徵的異常分數，通過從驗證殘差中校準的完全無監督閾值轉換為警報。<lb/>  
在與DC-VAE \cite{garcia2023onemodel}一起發布的TELCO數據集上，C-MTAD-GAT提高了事件級別的關聯性和逐點F1，同時生成的警報數量少於之前的圖注意力和基於VAE的基準。我們隨後將相同的系統應用於來自行動網路運營商的國家級無線接入和演進封包核心控制平面計數器數據，並在該網路中部署。運營商的反饋表明，這些警報是可操作的，並支持日常監控，顯示出在不依賴標記事件的情況下在不同領域的可擴展性。

##### **Unlearning What Matters: Token-Level Attribution for Precise Language Model Unlearning**
2605.00364v1 by Jiawei Wu, DouDou Zhou

Machine unlearning has emerged as a critical capability for addressing privacy, safety, and regulatory concerns in large language models (LLMs). Existing methods operate at the sequence level, applying uniform updates across all tokens despite only a subset encoding the knowledge targeted for removal. This introduces gradient noise, degrades utility, and leads to suboptimal forgetting. We propose TokenUnlearn, a token-level attribution framework that identifies and selectively targets critical tokens. Our approach combines knowledge-aware signals via masking, and entropy-aware signals to yield importance scores for precise token selection. We develop two complementary strategies: hard selection, applying unlearning only to high-importance tokens, and soft weighting, modulating gradient contributions based on importance scores. Both extend existing methods to token-level variants. Theoretical analysis shows token-level selection improves gradient signal-to-noise ratio. Experiments on TOFU and WMDP benchmarks across three model architectures demonstrate consistent improvements over sequence-level baselines in both forgetting effectiveness and utility preservation.

摘要：機器遺忘已成為解決大型語言模型（LLMs）中的隱私、安全和監管問題的關鍵能力。現有方法在序列層面運作，對所有標記應用統一更新，儘管只有一部分編碼了目標移除的知識。這引入了梯度噪聲，降低了效用，並導致次優的遺忘。我們提出了TokenUnlearn，一個標記級的歸因框架，能夠識別並選擇性地針對關鍵標記。我們的方法結合了通過遮罩獲得的知識感知信號和熵感知信號，以產生精確標記選擇的重要性分數。我們開發了兩種互補策略：硬選擇，僅對高重要性標記應用遺忘，以及軟加權，根據重要性分數調節梯度貢獻。這兩者將現有方法擴展到標記級變體。理論分析顯示，標記級選擇改善了梯度信號與噪聲的比率。在TOFU和WMDP基準上對三種模型架構的實驗顯示，在遺忘有效性和效用保留方面，相較於序列級基準有一致的改善。

##### **Making Every Verified Token Count: Adaptive Verification for MoE Speculative Decoding**
2605.00342v1 by Lehan Pan, Ziyang Tao, Ruoyu Pang, Xiao Wang, Jianjun Zhao, Yanyong Zhang

Tree-based speculative decoding accelerates autoregressive generation by verifying multiple draft candidates in parallel, but this advantage weakens for sparse Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models. As the draft tree grows, different branches activate different experts, expanding the union of activated experts and substantially increasing target-side verification cost. We propose EVICT, a training-free, hyperparameter-free, and lossless adaptive verification method for MoE speculative decoding. EVICT makes every verified token count by truncating the draft tree before target verification and retaining only the cost-effective prefix. It leverages fine-grained drafter signals to estimate candidate benefit, combines them with offline-profiled verification cost, and remains highly compatible with the high-performance graph-based serving framework SGLang. Extensive experiments on diverse MoE backbones and benchmarks show that EVICT achieves up to 2.35x speedup over autoregressive decoding and an average 1.21x speedup over the state-of-the-art baseline EAGLE-3, while significantly reducing unnecessary expert activations during verification.

摘要：樹狀的推測解碼透過並行驗證多個草稿候選者來加速自回歸生成，但這一優勢在稀疏的專家混合模型（MoE）中減弱。隨著草稿樹的增長，不同的分支激活不同的專家，擴大了激活專家的聯集，並大幅增加了目標端的驗證成本。我們提出了EVICT，一種無需訓練、無需超參數且無損的自適應驗證方法，用於MoE推測解碼。EVICT通過在目標驗證之前截斷草稿樹並僅保留成本效益高的前綴，使每個已驗證的標記都能發揮作用。它利用細粒度的草擬者信號來估算候選者的效益，並將其與離線配置的驗證成本相結合，並且與高性能的基於圖的服務框架SGLang高度兼容。在多樣的MoE骨幹和基準上的廣泛實驗顯示，EVICT在自回歸解碼上實現了高達2.35倍的加速，並在最先進的基準EAGLE-3上平均實現了1.21倍的加速，同時在驗證過程中顯著減少了不必要的專家激活。

##### **Beyond Visual Fidelity: Benchmarking Super-Resolution Models for Large-Scale Remote Sensing Imagery via Downstream Task Integration**
2605.00310v1 by Zhili Li, Kangyang Chai, Zhihao Wang, Xiaowei Jia, Yanhua Li, Gengchen Mai, Sergii Skakun, Dinesh Manocha, Yiqun Xie

Super-resolution (SR) techniques have made major advances in reconstructing high-resolution images from low-resolution inputs. The increased resolution provides visual enhancement and utility for monitoring tasks. In particular, SR has been increasingly developed for satellite-based Earth observation, with applications in urban planning, agriculture, ecology, and disaster response. However, existing SR studies and benchmarks typically use fidelity metrics such as PSNR or SSIM, whereas the true utility of super-resolved images lies in supporting downstream tasks such as land cover classification, biomass estimation, and change detection. To bridge this gap, we introduce GeoSR-Bench, a downstream task-integrated SR benchmark dataset to evaluate SR models beyond fidelity metrics. GeoSR-Bench comprises spatially co-located, temporally aligned, and quality-controlled image pairs from about 36,000 locations across diverse land covers, spanning resolutions from 500m to 0.6m. To the best of our knowledge, GeoSR-Bench is the first SR benchmark that directly connects improved image resolution from SR models with downstream Earth monitoring tasks, including land cover segmentation, infrastructure mapping, and biophysical variable estimation. Using GeoSR-Bench, we benchmark GAN, transformer, neural operator, and diffusion-based SR models on perceptual quality and downstream task performance. We conduct experiments with 270 settings, covering 2 cross-platform SR tasks, 9 SR models, 3 downstream task models, and 5 downstream tasks for each SR task. The results show that improvements in traditional SR metrics often do not correlate with gains in task performance, and the correlations can be negative, indicating that these metrics provide limited guidance for selecting superior models for downstream tasks. This reveals the need to integrate downstream tasks into SR model development and evaluation.

摘要：超解析度（SR）技術在從低解析度輸入重建高解析度圖像方面取得了重大進展。<lb/>提高的解析度為監測任務提供了視覺增強和實用性。<lb/>特別是，SR 在基於衛星的地球觀測中得到了越來越多的發展，應用於城市規劃、農業、生態學和災害應對等領域。<lb/>然而，現有的 SR 研究和基準通常使用 PSNR 或 SSIM 等保真度指標，而超解析圖像的真正實用性在於支持下游任務，如土地覆蓋分類、生物量估算和變化檢測。<lb/>為了彌補這一差距，我們引入了 GeoSR-Bench，一個集成下游任務的 SR 基準數據集，以評估 SR 模型超越保真度指標的表現。<lb/>GeoSR-Bench 包含來自約 36,000 個地點的空間共置、時間對齊和質量控制的圖像對，涵蓋從 500 米到 0.6 米的多樣土地覆蓋解析度。<lb/>據我們所知，GeoSR-Bench 是第一個直接將 SR 模型改善的圖像解析度與下游地球監測任務（包括土地覆蓋分割、基礎設施映射和生物物理變量估算）聯繫起來的 SR 基準。<lb/>使用 GeoSR-Bench，我們在感知質量和下游任務性能上對 GAN、Transformer、神經運算子和基於擴散的 SR 模型進行基準測試。<lb/>我們進行了 270 種設置的實驗，涵蓋 2 種跨平台 SR 任務、9 種 SR 模型、3 種下游任務模型，以及每個 SR 任務的 5 種下游任務。<lb/>結果顯示，傳統 SR 指標的改善通常與任務性能的提升無關，且相關性可能為負，這表明這些指標對於選擇優越模型以應對下游任務的指導意義有限。<lb/>這揭示了將下游任務整合到 SR 模型開發和評估中的必要性。

##### **Jailbroken Frontier Models Retain Their Capabilities**
2605.00267v1 by Daniel Zhu, Zihan Wang, Jenny Bao, Jerry Wei

As language model safeguards become more robust, attackers are pushed toward developing increasingly complex jailbreaks. Prior work has found that this complexity imposes a "jailbreak tax" that degrades the target model's task performance. We show that this tax scales inversely with model capability and that the most advanced jailbreaks effectively yield no reduction in model capabilities. Evaluating 28 jailbreaks on five benchmarks across Claude models ranging in capability from Haiku 4.5 to Opus 4.6, we find Haiku 4.5 loses an average of 33.1% on benchmark performance when jailbroken, while Opus 4.6 at max thinking effort loses only 7.7%. We also observe that across all models, reasoning-heavy tasks display considerably more degradation than knowledge-recall tasks. Finally, Boundary Point Jailbreaking, currently the strongest jailbreak against deployed classifiers, achieves near-perfect classifier evasion with near-zero degradation across safeguarded models. We recommend that safety cases for frontier models should not rely on a meaningful capability degradation from jailbreaks.

摘要：隨著語言模型的安全措施變得更加健全，攻擊者被迫開發越來越複雜的越獄手段。先前的研究發現，這種複雜性會施加一種「越獄稅」，從而降低目標模型的任務表現。我們顯示這種稅收與模型能力呈反比，最先進的越獄手段實際上不會有效降低模型能力。我們對五個基準測試中的28個越獄手段進行評估，這些基準測試涵蓋了從 Haiku 4.5 到 Opus 4.6 的 Claude 模型，我們發現 Haiku 4.5 在越獄後基準表現平均損失 33.1%，而 Opus 4.6 在最大思考努力下僅損失 7.7%。我們還觀察到，在所有模型中，重推理任務的性能下降顯著高於知識回憶任務。最後，邊界點越獄（Boundary Point Jailbreaking），目前對已部署分類器的最強越獄手段，實現了近乎完美的分類器逃避，並在受到保護的模型中幾乎沒有性能下降。我們建議，對前沿模型的安全案例不應依賴於越獄所帶來的顯著能力下降。

##### **Retrieval-Augmented Reasoning for Chartered Accountancy**
2605.00257v1 by Jatin Gupta, Akhil Sharma, Saransh Singhania, Ali Imam Abidi

The inception of Large Language Models (LLMs) has catalyzed AI adoption in the finance sector, yet their reliability in complex, jurisdiction-specific tasks like Indian Chartered Accountancy (CA) remains limited. The models display difficulty in executing numerical tasks which require multiple steps while also needing advanced knowledge about legal regulations and the method of scaling their operations is not feasible in settings which have limited access to resources. We present CA-ThinkFlow as a parameter-efficient Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) framework which operates with a 14B, 4-bit-quantized reasoning model, 14B-DeepSeek-R1, and a layout-aware Docling extraction system which maintains document structure during extraction. CA-ThinkFlow uses a basic RAG method which automatically adds retrieved information into the prompt, while it depends on the model's built-in Chain-of-Thought (CoT) functions to create context and produce correct answers. The system we developed system operates at performance levels which match large proprietary models when we tested it on the multi-level CA-Ben benchmark, achieving Scholastic Reliability Coefficient (SRC) results which equal 68.75\% of GPT-4o and Claude 3.5 Sonnet. The framework shows high efficiency and strength in handling parameters, but essential reasoning abilities fail to process complex regulatory texts which exist in fields such as Taxation.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）的出現促進了金融領域的人工智慧採用，但它們在複雜的、特定於法域的任務（如印度特許會計師（CA））中的可靠性仍然有限。這些模型在執行需要多步驟的數字任務時顯示出困難，同時也需要對法律法規有深入的了解，而在資源有限的環境中擴展其運作的方法並不可行。我們提出了CA-ThinkFlow，這是一個參數高效的檢索增強生成（RAG）框架，使用一個14B、4位量化的推理模型14B-DeepSeek-R1，以及一個在提取過程中保持文檔結構的佈局感知Docling提取系統。CA-ThinkFlow使用一種基本的RAG方法，自動將檢索到的信息添加到提示中，同時依賴模型內建的思維鏈（CoT）功能來創建上下文並產生正確答案。我們開發的系統在多層CA-Ben基準測試中表現出與大型專有模型相匹配的性能水平，實現了68.75\%的學術可靠性係數（SRC）結果，與GPT-4o和Claude 3.5 Sonnet相等。該框架在處理參數方面顯示出高效率和強大能力，但基本的推理能力無法處理存在於稅收等領域的複雜法規文本。

##### **LLM as Clinical Graph Structure Refiner: Enhancing Representation Learning in EEG Seizure Diagnosis**
2604.28178v1 by Lincan Li, Zheng Chen, Yushun Dong

Electroencephalogram (EEG) signals are vital for automated seizure detection, but their inherent noise makes robust representation learning challenging. Existing graph construction methods, whether correlation-based or learning-based, often generate redundant or irrelevant edges due to the noisy nature of EEG data. This significantly impairs the quality of graph representation and limits downstream task performance. Motivated by the remarkable reasoning and contextual understanding capabilities of large language models (LLMs), we explore the idea of using LLMs as graph edge refiners. Specifically, we propose a two-stage framework: we first verify that LLM-based edge refinement can effectively identify and remove redundant connections, leading to significant improvements in seizure detection accuracy and more meaningful graph structures. Building on this insight, we further develop a robust solution where the initial graph is constructed using a Transformer-based edge predictor and multilayer perceptron, assigning probability scores to potential edges and applying a threshold to determine their existence. The LLM then acts as an edge set refiner, making informed decisions based on both textual and statistical features of node pairs to validate the remaining connections. Extensive experiments on TUSZ dataset demonstrate that our LLM-refined graph learning framework not only enhances task performance but also yields cleaner and more interpretable graph representations.

摘要：腦電圖 (EEG) 信號對於自動癲癇發作檢測至關重要，但其固有的噪聲使得穩健的表示學習變得具有挑戰性。現有的圖構建方法，無論是基於相關性還是基於學習，通常因為EEG數據的噪聲特性而產生冗餘或不相關的邊。這顯著損害了圖表示的質量，並限制了下游任務的表現。受到大型語言模型 (LLMs) 卓越的推理和上下文理解能力的啟發，我們探索了將LLMs用作圖邊緣精煉器的想法。具體而言，我們提出了一個兩階段的框架：首先，我們驗證基於LLM的邊緣精煉可以有效識別和移除冗餘連接，從而顯著提高癲癇檢測的準確性並形成更有意義的圖結構。在此基礎上，我們進一步開發了一個穩健的解決方案，其中初始圖是使用基於Transformer的邊緣預測器和多層感知器構建的，為潛在邊分配概率分數並應用閾值來確定其存在性。然後，LLM作為邊緣集的精煉器，根據節點對的文本和統計特徵做出明智的決策，以驗證剩餘的連接。在TUSZ數據集上進行的廣泛實驗表明，我們的LLM精煉圖學習框架不僅提高了任務表現，還產生了更乾淨和更具可解釋性的圖表示。

##### **Intern-Atlas: A Methodological Evolution Graph as Research Infrastructure for AI Scientists**
2604.28158v2 by Yujun Wu, Dongxu Zhang, Xinchen Li, Jinhang Xu, Yiling Duan, Yumou Liu, Jiabao Pan, Qiyuan Zhu, Xuanhe Zhou, Jingxuan Wei, Siyuan Li, Jintao Chen, Conghui He, Cheng Tan

Existing research infrastructure is fundamentally document-centric, providing citation links between papers but lacking explicit representations of methodological evolution. In particular, it does not capture the structured relationships that explain how and why research methods emerge, adapt, and build upon one another. With the rise of AI-driven research agents as a new class of consumers of scientific knowledge, this limitation becomes increasingly consequential, as such agents cannot reliably reconstruct method evolution topologies from unstructured text. We introduce Intern-Atlas, a methodological evolution graph that automatically identifies method-level entities, infers lineage relationships among methodologies, and captures the bottlenecks that drive transitions between successive innovations. Built from 1,030,314 papers spanning AI conferences, journals, and arXiv preprints, the resulting graph comprises 9,410,201 semantically typed edges, each grounded in verbatim source evidence, forming a queryable causal network of methodological development. To operationalize this structure, we further propose a self-guided temporal tree search algorithm for constructing evolution chains that trace the progression of methods over time. We evaluate the quality of the resulting graph against expert-curated ground-truth evolution chains and observe strong alignment. In addition, we demonstrate that Intern-Atlas enables downstream applications in idea evaluation and automated idea generation. We position methodological evolution graphs as a foundational data layer for the emerging automated scientific discovery.

摘要：現有的研究基礎設施基本上是以文檔為中心，提供論文之間的引用鏈接，但缺乏對方法論演變的明確表現。<lb/>特別是，它無法捕捉解釋研究方法如何以及為何出現、適應和相互建立的結構性關係。<lb/>隨著以 AI 驅動的研究代理作為科學知識新消費者類別的興起，這一限制變得越來越重要，因為這些代理無法可靠地從非結構化文本中重建方法演變拓撲。<lb/>我們介紹了 Intern-Atlas，一個方法論演變圖，自動識別方法層級實體，推斷方法論之間的血統關係，並捕捉推動連續創新之間轉變的瓶頸。<lb/>該圖由 1,030,314 篇涵蓋 AI 會議、期刊和 arXiv 預印本的論文構建而成，最終圖形包含 9,410,201 條語義類型的邊，每條邊都基於逐字的來源證據，形成一個可查詢的因果網絡，描述方法論的發展。<lb/>為了使這一結構具體化，我們進一步提出了一種自導式時間樹搜索算法，用於構建演變鏈，追溯方法隨時間的演進。<lb/>我們將結果圖的質量與專家策劃的真實演變鏈進行評估，並觀察到強烈的一致性。<lb/>此外，我們展示了 Intern-Atlas 能夠促進想法評估和自動化想法生成的下游應用。<lb/>我們將方法論演變圖定位為新興自動化科學發現的基礎數據層。

##### **NorBERTo: A ModernBERT Model Trained for Portuguese with 331 Billion Tokens Corpus**
2605.00086v1 by Enzo S. N. Silva, Pablo B. Costa, Raphael C. Vlasman, Rosimeire P. Costa, Henrique L. P. Silva, Lucas F. A. O. Pellicer, Guilherme Rinaldo, Renato A. Almeida, Darian S. R. Rabbani, Cinthya O. Oestreich, Vinicius F. Caridá

High-quality corpora are essential for advancing Natural Language Processing (NLP) in Portuguese. NorBERTo is trained on Aurora-PT, a newly curated Brazilian Portuguese corpus comprising 331 billion GPT-2 tokens collected from diverse web sources and existing multilingual datasets. To the best of our knowledge, Aurora-PT is currently the largest openly available monolingual Portuguese corpus, surpassing previous resources. NorBERTo provides a modern, mid-sized encoder designed for realistic deployment scenarios: it is straight-forward to fine-tune, efficient to serve, and well suited as a backbone for retrieval-augmented generation and other downstream Portuguese NLP systems.

##### **DEFault++: Automated Fault Detection, Categorization, and Diagnosis for Transformer Architectures**
2604.28118v1 by Sigma Jahan, Saurabh Singh Rajput, Tushar Sharma, Mohammad Masudur Rahman

Transformer models are widely deployed in critical AI applications, yet faults in their attention mechanisms, projections, and other internal components often degrade behavior silently without raising runtime errors. Existing fault diagnosis techniques often target generic deep neural networks and cannot identify which transformer component is responsible for an observed symptom. In this article, we present DEFault++, a hierarchical learning-based diagnostic technique that operates at three level of abstraction: it detects whether a fault is present, classifies it into one of 12 transformer-specific fault categories (covering both attention-internal mechanisms and surrounding architectural components), and identifies the underlying root cause from up to 45 mechanisms. To facilitate both training and evaluation, we construct DEFault-bench, a benchmark of 3,739 labeled instances obtained through systematic mutation testing. These instances are created across seven transformer models and nine downstream tasks using DEForm, a transformer-specific mutation technique we developed for this purpose. DEFault++ measures runtime behavior at the level of individual transformer components. It organizes these measurements through a Fault Propagation Graph (FPG) derived from the transformer architecture. It then produces an interpretable diagnosis using prototype matching combined with supervised contrastive learning. On DEFault-bench, DEFault++ exceeds an AUROC of 0.96 for detection and a Macro-F1 of 0.85 for both categorization and root-cause diagnosis on encoder and decoder architectures. In a developer study with 21 practitioners, the accuracy of choosing correct repair actions increased from 57.1% without support to 83.3% when using DEFault++.

摘要：Transformer模型在關鍵的人工智慧應用中被廣泛部署，但其注意力機制、投影和其他內部組件中的故障往往會在不引發運行時錯誤的情況下靜默地降低行為表現。現有的故障診斷技術通常針對通用深度神經網絡，無法識別出導致觀察到的症狀的具體Transformer組件。在本文中，我們提出了DEFault++，這是一種基於分層學習的診斷技術，運作於三個抽象層級：它檢測故障是否存在，將其分類為12個特定於Transformer的故障類別（涵蓋內部注意力機制和周邊架構組件），並從多達45種機制中識別出根本原因。為了促進訓練和評估，我們構建了DEFault-bench，這是一個通過系統性變異測試獲得的3,739個標記實例的基準。這些實例是通過我們為此目的開發的特定於Transformer的變異技術DEForm，在七個Transformer模型和九個下游任務中創建的。DEFault++在個別Transformer組件的層面上測量運行時行為。它通過從Transformer架構衍生的故障傳播圖（FPG）組織這些測量。然後，它使用原型匹配結合監督對比學習生成可解釋的診斷。在DEFault-bench上，DEFault++在檢測方面超過了0.96的AUROC，在編碼器和解碼器架構上，分類和根本原因診斷的Macro-F1達到了0.85。在一項針對21名從業者的開發者研究中，選擇正確修復行動的準確率從沒有支持的57.1%提高到使用DEFault++時的83.3%。

##### **What Makes a Good Terminal-Agent Benchmark Task: A Guideline for Adversarial, Difficult, and Legible Evaluation Design**
2604.28093v1 by Ivan Bercovich

Terminal-agent benchmarks have become a primary signal for measuring the coding and system-administration capabilities of large language models. As the market for evaluation environments grows, so does the pressure to ship tasks quickly, often without thorough adversarial review of the verification logic. This paper is a guideline for writing good benchmark tasks, drawn from over a year of contributing to and reviewing tasks for Terminal Bench. Most people write benchmark tasks the way they write prompts. They shouldn't. A prompt is designed to help the agent succeed; a benchmark is designed to find out if it can. We argue that good tasks are adversarial, difficult, and legible, and that a large class of common failure modes -- AI-generated instructions, over-prescriptive specifications, clerical difficulty, oracle solutions that assume hidden knowledge, tests that validate the wrong things, and reward-hackable environments -- are predictable consequences of treating task authoring as prompt authoring. We catalog these failure modes, argue that real difficulty is conceptual rather than environmental, and discuss recent empirical evidence that over 15% of tasks in popular terminal-agent benchmarks are reward-hackable. We hope this serves as a useful reference for benchmark maintainers, task contributors, and researchers using benchmark scores as evidence.

摘要：終端代理基準已成為衡量大型語言模型編碼和系統管理能力的主要指標。隨著評估環境市場的增長，快速交付任務的壓力也隨之增加，通常在沒有徹底對驗證邏輯進行對抗性審查的情況下進行。本文是撰寫良好基準任務的指導方針，基於一年多來對終端基準任務的貢獻和審查。大多數人撰寫基準任務的方式與撰寫提示的方式相同，但這樣不應該。提示旨在幫助代理成功；基準旨在找出它是否能夠成功。我們認為良好的任務應具備對抗性、困難性和可讀性，並且一大類常見的失敗模式——AI生成的指令、過於具體的規範、文書難度、假設隱藏知識的神諭解決方案、驗證錯誤事物的測試，以及可獎勵操控的環境——是將任務創作視為提示創作的可預測後果。我們對這些失敗模式進行了編目，並主張真正的困難是概念性的而非環境性的，並討論了最近的實證證據，顯示在流行的終端代理基準中超過15%的任務是可獎勵操控的。我們希望這能成為基準維護者、任務貢獻者和使用基準分數作為證據的研究人員的有用參考。

##### **Towards Neuro-symbolic Causal Rule Synthesis, Verification, and Evaluation Grounded in Legal and Safety Principles**
2604.28087v1 by Zainab Rehan, Christian Medeiros Adriano, Sona Ghahremani, Holger Giese

Rule-based systems remain central in safety-critical domains but often struggle with scalability, brittleness, and goal misspecification. These limitations can lead to reward hacking and failures in formal verification, as AI systems tend to optimize for narrow objectives. In previous research, we developed a neuro-symbolic causal framework that integrates first-order logic abduction trees, structural causal models, and deep reinforcement learning within a MAPE-K loop to provide explainable adaptations under distribution shifts. In this paper, we extend that framework by introducing a meta-level layer designed to mitigate goal misspecification and support scalable rule maintenance. This layer consists of a Goal/Rule Synthesizer and a Rule Verification Engine, which iteratively refine a formal rule theory from high-level natural-language goals and principles provided by human experts. The synthesis pipeline employs large language models (LLMs) to: (1) decompose goals into candidate causes, (2) consolidate semantics to remove redundancies, (3) translate them into candidate first-order rules, and (4) compose necessary and sufficient causal sets. The verification pipeline then performs (1) syntax and schema validation, (2) logical consistency analysis, and (3) safety and invariant checks before integrating verified rules into the knowledge base. We evaluated our approach with a proof-of-concept implementation in two autonomous driving scenarios. Results indicate that, given human-specified goals and principles, the pipeline can successfully derive minimal necessary and sufficient rule sets and formalize them as logical constraints. These findings suggest that the pipeline supports incremental, modular, and traceable rule synthesis grounded in established legal and safety principles.

摘要：基於規則的系統在安全關鍵領域仍然是核心，但常常在可擴展性、脆弱性和目標錯誤指定方面遇到困難。這些限制可能導致獎勵駭客行為和正式驗證失敗，因為AI系統傾向於優化狹隘的目標。在先前的研究中，我們開發了一個神經符號因果框架，該框架整合了第一階邏輯推理樹、結構因果模型和深度強化學習，並在MAPE-K循環中提供可解釋的適應，以應對分佈變化。在本文中，我們通過引入一個元層來擴展該框架，旨在減輕目標錯誤指定並支持可擴展的規則維護。這一層由目標/規則合成器和規則驗證引擎組成，這些組件迭代地從人類專家提供的高級自然語言目標和原則中提煉出正式的規則理論。合成管道利用大型語言模型（LLMs）來：(1) 將目標分解為候選原因，(2) 整合語義以消除冗餘，(3) 將其轉化為候選的第一階規則，並 (4) 組合必要且充分的因果集合。然後，驗證管道執行 (1) 語法和結構驗證，(2) 邏輯一致性分析，以及 (3) 安全性和不變性檢查，然後將驗證過的規則整合到知識庫中。我們在兩個自動駕駛場景中通過概念驗證實現評估了我們的方法。結果表明，給定人類指定的目標和原則，該管道可以成功推導出最小必要且充分的規則集，並將其形式化為邏輯約束。這些發現表明，該管道支持基於既定法律和安全原則的增量、模塊化和可追蹤的規則合成。

##### **Design Structure Matrix Modularization with Large Language Models**
2604.28018v1 by Shuo Jiang, Jianxi Luo

Design Structure Matrix (DSM) modularization, the task of partitioning system elements into cohesive modules, is a fundamental combinatorial challenge in engineering design. Traditional methods treat modularization as a pure graph optimization, without access to the engineering context embedded in the system. Building on prior work on LLM-based combinatorial optimization for DSM sequencing, this paper extends the method to modularization across five cases and three backbone LLMs. Our method achieves near-reference quality within 30 iterations without requiring specialized optimization code. Counterintuitively, domain knowledge, beneficial in sequencing, consistently impairs performance on more complex DSMs. We attribute this to semantic misalignment between the LLM's functional priors and the purely structural optimization objective, and propose the semantic-alignment hypothesis as a testable condition governing knowledge effectiveness with LLMs. Ablation studies identify the most effective input representation, objective formulation, and solution pool design for practical deployment. ##### **Splitting Assumption-Based Argumentation Frameworks**
2604.27964v1 by Giovanni Buraglio, Wolfgang Dvorak, Stefan Woltran

Assumption-Based Argumentation (ABA) is a well-established formalism for modelling and reasoning over debates, with a wide range of applications. However, the high computational complexity of core reasoning tasks in ABA poses a significant challenge for its applicability. This issue is further aggravated when ABA frameworks (ABAFs) are instantiated into graph-based argumentation formalisms, such as Dung's Argumentation Frameworks (AFs) and Argumentation Frameworks with Collective Attacks (SETAFs). In knowledge representation and reasoning, a key strategy to address computational intractability is to optimise reasoning over a given knowledge base through divide-and-conquer algorithms. A paradigmatic example of this approach is splitting, where extensions of a given framework are computed incrementally, by restricting the search space to sub-frameworks only, and then combining the obtained results. This approach has been successfully applied to AFs, for which also a parametrised version has been introduced under stable semantics. However, the exponential growth produced by the instantiation might undermine the usefulness of splitting on the argument graphs induced by ABAFs. To address this issue, our work investigates the concept of splitting on the knowledge base rather than on its graph-based instantiation. Furthermore, we generalise splitting to its parametrised version for ABAFs.

摘要：假設基礎論證（ABA）是一種成熟的形式主義，用於建模和推理辯論，應用範圍廣泛。<lb/>然而，ABA中的核心推理任務的高計算複雜性對其適用性構成了重大挑戰。<lb/>當ABA框架（ABAFs）被實例化為基於圖的論證形式主義時，這一問題進一步加劇，例如鄧的論證框架（AFs）和具有集體攻擊的論證框架（SETAFs）。<lb/>在知識表示和推理中，解決計算不可處理性的關鍵策略是通過分而治之算法來優化對給定知識庫的推理。<lb/>這一方法的典型例子是拆分，其中通過將搜索空間限制為子框架，逐步計算給定框架的擴展，然後合併獲得的結果。<lb/>這一方法已成功應用於AFs，並且在穩定語義下也引入了一個參數化版本。<lb/>然而，實例化所產生的指數增長可能會削弱拆分在ABAFs所誘導的論證圖上的有效性。<lb/>為了解決這一問題，我們的工作探討了在知識庫上進行拆分的概念，而不是在其基於圖的實例化上。<lb/>此外，我們將拆分推廣到其ABAFs的參數化版本。

##### **LLMs as ASP Programmers: Self-Correction Enables Task-Agnostic Nonmonotonic Reasoning**
2604.27960v1 by Adam Ishay, Joohyung Lee

Recent large language models (LLMs) have achieved impressive reasoning milestones but continue to struggle with high computational costs, logical inconsistencies, and sharp performance degradation on high-complexity problems. While neuro-symbolic methods attempt to mitigate these issues by coupling LLMs with symbolic reasoners, existing approaches typically rely on monotonic logics (e.g., SMT) that cannot represent defeasible reasoning -- essential components of human cognition. We present "LLM+ASP," a framework that translates natural language into Answer Set Programming (ASP), a nonmonotonic formalism based on stable model semantics. Unlike prior "LLM+ASP" approaches that require manually authored knowledge modules, domain-specific prompts, or evaluation restricted to single problem classes, our framework operates without any per-task engineering and applies uniformly across diverse reasoning tasks. Our system utilizes an automated self-correction loop where structured feedback from the ASP solver enables iterative refinement. Evaluating across six diverse benchmarks, we demonstrate that: (1) stable model semantics allow LLMs to naturally express default rules and exceptions, outperforming SMT-based alternatives by significant margins on nonmonotonic tasks; (2) iterative self-correction is the primary driver of performance, effectively replacing the need for handcrafted domain knowledge; (3) compact in-context reference guides substantially outperform verbose documentation, revealing a "context rot" phenomenon where excessive context hinders constraint adherence.

摘要：最近的大型語言模型（LLMs）在推理方面取得了令人印象深刻的里程碑，但仍然面臨高計算成本、邏輯不一致性以及在高複雜性問題上的性能急劇下降等挑戰。雖然神經符號方法試圖通過將LLMs與符號推理器結合來減輕這些問題，但現有的方法通常依賴於單調邏輯（例如，SMT），這無法表示可推翻的推理——這是人類認知的基本組成部分。我們提出了“LLM+ASP”，一個將自然語言轉換為答案集編程（ASP）的框架，這是一種基於穩定模型語義的非單調形式主義。與之前需要手動編寫知識模塊、特定領域提示或限制在單一問題類別的評估的“LLM+ASP”方法不同，我們的框架在無需任何每個任務的工程的情況下運作，並且在各種推理任務中均可均勻應用。我們的系統利用自動自我修正循環，其中來自ASP求解器的結構化反饋使得迭代改進成為可能。在六個不同的基準測試中進行評估，我們證明了：（1）穩定模型語義允許LLMs自然表達默認規則和例外，在非單調任務中顯著超越基於SMT的替代方案；（2）迭代自我修正是性能的主要驅動力，有效取代了手工製作的領域知識的需求；（3）緊湊的上下文參考指南顯著超越冗長的文檔，揭示了“上下文衰退”現象，其中過多的上下文妨礙了約束的遵守。

##### **DPN-LE: Dual Personality Neuron Localization and Editing for Large Language Models**
2604.27929v1 by Lifan Zheng, Xue Yang, Jiawei Chen, Chenyan Wu, Jingyuan Zhang, Fanheng Kong, Xinyi Zeng, Xiang Chen, Yu Tian

With the widespread adoption of large language models (LLMs), understanding their personality representation mechanisms has become critical. As a novel paradigm in Personality Editing, most existing methods employ neuron-editing to locate and modify LLM neurons, requiring changes to numerous neurons and leading to significant performance degradation. This raises a fundamental question: Are all modified neurons directly related to personality representation? In this work, we investigate and quantify this specificity through assessments of general capability impact and representation-level patterns. We find that: 1) Current methods can change personalities but reduce overall performance. 2) Neurons are multifunctional, connecting personality traits and general knowledge. 3) Opposing personality traits demonstrate distinctly mutually exclusive representation patterns. Motivated by these findings, we propose DPN-LE (Dual Personality Neuron Localization and Editing), which identifies personality-specific neurons by contrasting MLP activations between high-trait and low-trait samples. DPN-LE constructs layer-wise steering vectors and applies dual-criterion filtering based on Cohen's $d$ effect size and activation magnitude to isolate mutually exclusive neuron subsets. Sparse linear intervention on these neurons enables precise personality control at inference time. Using only 1,000 contrastive sample pairs per trait, DPN-LE intervenes on $\sim$0.5\% of neurons while achieving competitive personality control and substantially better capability preservation across reasoning tasks. Experiments on LLaMA-3-8B-Instruct and Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct demonstrate the effectiveness and generalizability of our approach.

摘要：隨著大型語言模型（LLMs）的廣泛應用，理解其人格表徵機制變得至關重要。作為人格編輯中的一種新穎範式，大多數現有方法採用神經元編輯來定位和修改LLM神經元，這需要改變大量神經元，並導致顯著的性能下降。這引發了一個根本問題：所有被修改的神經元是否都與人格表徵直接相關？在本研究中，我們通過對一般能力影響和表徵層級模式的評估來調查和量化這種特異性。我們發現：1）當前方法可以改變人格，但會降低整體性能。2）神經元是多功能的，連接人格特徵和一般知識。3）對立的人格特徵顯示出明顯的互斥表徵模式。受到這些發現的啟發，我們提出了DPN-LE（雙人格神經元定位與編輯），通過對比高特徵和低特徵樣本之間的MLP激活來識別人格特定神經元。DPN-LE構建層級引導向量，並基於Cohen的$d$效應大小和激活幅度應用雙標準過濾，以隔離互斥的神經元子集。對這些神經元進行稀疏線性干預使得在推理時能夠精確控制人格。僅使用每個特徵1,000對對比樣本，DPN-LE對約0.5\%的神經元進行干預，同時實現了具有競爭力的人格控制，並在推理任務中顯著更好地保留能力。在LLaMA-3-8B-Instruct和Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct上的實驗證明了我們方法的有效性和普遍性。

##### **Training-Free Tunnel Defect Inspection and Engineering Interpretation via Visual Recalibration and Entity Reconstruction**
2604.27928v1 by Shipeng Liu, Liang Zhao, Dengfeng Chen, Zhanping Song

Tunnel inspection requires outputs that can support defect localization, measurement, severity grading, and engineering documentation. Existing training-free foundation-model pipelines usually stop at coarse open-vocabulary proposals, which are difficult to use directly in interference-heavy tunnel scenes. We propose a training-free framework TunnelMIND. Specifically, language-guided defect proposals are not treated as final outputs; instead, their spatial support is recalibrated at inference time through dense visual consistency, so that coarse semantic anchors can be transformed into more reliable prompts under tunnel-specific hard negatives. The resulting masks are further reconstructed into structured defect entities with category, location, geometry, severity, and context attributes, which are then mapped to retrieval-grounded explanation and engineering-readable report generation under expert knowledge constraints. On visible, GPR, and road defect tasks, TunnelMIND achieves F1 scores of 0.68, 0.78, and 0.72, respectively. Overall, TunnelMIND shows that training-free tunnel inspection can move beyond coarse localization toward structured defect evidence for engineering assessment.

摘要：隧道檢查需要能夠支持缺陷定位、測量、嚴重程度分級和工程文檔的輸出。現有的無需訓練的基礎模型管道通常停留在粗略的開放詞彙提議上，這在干擾較重的隧道場景中難以直接使用。我們提出了一個無需訓練的框架 TunnelMIND。具體而言，語言引導的缺陷提議並不被視為最終輸出；相反，它們的空間支持在推理時通過密集的視覺一致性進行重新校準，以便將粗略的語義錨點轉換為在隧道特定的困難負例下更可靠的提示。生成的掩碼進一步重建為結構化的缺陷實體，具有類別、位置、幾何形狀、嚴重程度和上下文屬性，然後在專家知識約束下映射到基於檢索的解釋和工程可讀報告生成。在可見、GPR 和道路缺陷任務中，TunnelMIND 分別達到了 0.68、0.78 和 0.72 的 F1 分數。總體而言，TunnelMIND 顯示無需訓練的隧道檢查可以超越粗略定位，朝向結構化的缺陷證據以進行工程評估。

##### **Geometry-Calibrated Conformal Abstention for Language Models**
2604.27914v1 by Rui Xu, Yi Chen, Sihong Xie, Hui Xiong

When language models lack relevant knowledge for a given query, they frequently generate plausible responses that can be hallucinations, rather than admitting being agnostic about the answer. Retraining models to reward admitting ignorance can lead to overly conservative behaviors and poor generalization due to scarce evaluation benchmarks. We propose a post hoc framework, Conformal Abstention (CA), adapted from conformal prediction (CP) to determine whether to abstain from answering a query. CA provides finite-sample guarantees on both the probability of participation (i.e., not abstaining) and the probability that the generated response is correct. Importantly, the abstention decision relies on prediction confidence rather than the non-conformity scores used in CP, which are intractable for open-ended generation. To better align prediction confidence with the model's ignorance, we introduce a calibration strategy using representation geometry within the model to measure knowledge involvement in shaping the response. Experiments demonstrate that we improve selective answering significantly with 75 percent conditional correctness.

摘要：當語言模型缺乏針對特定查詢的相關知識時，它們經常生成看似合理的回應，這些回應可能是幻覺，而不是承認對答案的無知。重新訓練模型以獎勵承認無知可能導致過於保守的行為和由於評估基準稀缺而造成的糟糕泛化。我們提出了一個事後框架，稱為符合性放棄（Conformal Abstention, CA），該框架改編自符合性預測（Conformal Prediction, CP），用於決定是否放棄回答查詢。CA 提供了有限樣本保證，涵蓋參與的概率（即不放棄）和生成的回應正確的概率。重要的是，放棄決策依賴於預測信心，而不是 CP 中使用的非符合性分數，後者對於開放式生成來說是不可處理的。為了更好地將預測信心與模型的無知對齊，我們引入了一種校準策略，利用模型內的表示幾何來測量知識在塑造回應中的參與程度。實驗表明，我們在有條件的正確性達到 75% 的情況下顯著改善了選擇性回答。

##### **Graph World Models: Concepts, Taxonomy, and Future Directions**
2604.27895v1 by Jiawei Liu, Senqiao Yang, Mingjun Wang, Yu Wang, Bei Yu

As one of the mainstream models of artificial intelligence, world models allow agents to learn the representation of the environment for efficient prediction and planning. However, classical world models based on flat tensors face several key problems, including noise sensitivity, error accumulation and weak reasoning. To address these limitations, many recent studies use graph structure to decompose the environment into entity nodes and interactive edges, and model virtual environments in a structured space. This paper systematically formalizes and unifies these emerging graph-based works under the concept of graph world models (GWMs). To the best of our knowledge, GWMs have not yet been explicitly defined and surveyed as a unified research paradigm. Furthermore, we propose a taxonomy based on relational inductive biases (RIB), categorizing GWMs by the specific structural priors they inject: (1) spatial RIB for topological abstraction; (2) physical RIB for dynamic simulation; and (3) logical RIB for causal and semantic reasoning. For each model category, we outline the key design principles, summarize representative models, and conduct comparative analyses. We further discuss open challenges and future directions, including dynamic graph adaptation, probabilistic relational dynamics, multi-granularity inductive biases, and the need for dedicated benchmarks and evaluation metrics for GWMs.

摘要：作為人工智慧的主流模型之一，世界模型允許代理學習環境的表示，以便進行有效的預測和規劃。<lb/>然而，基於平面張量的經典世界模型面臨幾個關鍵問題，包括噪音敏感性、錯誤累積和推理能力不足。<lb/>為了應對這些限制，許多最近的研究使用圖結構將環境分解為實體節點和互動邊，並在結構化空間中建模虛擬環境。<lb/>本文系統地形式化並統一這些新興的基於圖的研究，提出圖世界模型（GWMs）的概念。<lb/>據我們所知，GWMs尚未明確定義和調查作為一個統一的研究範式。<lb/>此外，我們提出了一個基於關係歸納偏見（RIB）的分類法，根據它們注入的特定結構先驗來對GWMs進行分類：<lb/>(1) 用於拓撲抽象的空間RIB；<lb/>(2) 用於動態模擬的物理RIB；<lb/>(3) 用於因果和語義推理的邏輯RIB。<lb/>對於每個模型類別，我們概述了關鍵設計原則，總結了代表性模型，並進行了比較分析。<lb/>我們進一步討論了開放挑戰和未來方向，包括動態圖適應、概率關係動態、多粒度歸納偏見，以及對GWMs專門基準和評估指標的需求。

##### **ObjectGraph: From Document Injection to Knowledge Traversal -- A Native File Format for the Agentic Era**
2604.27820v1 by Mohit Dubey, Open Gigantic

Every document format in existence was designed for a human reader moving linearly through text. Autonomous LLM agents do not read - they retrieve. This fundamental mismatch forces agents to inject entire documents into their context window, wasting tokens on irrelevant content, compounding state across multi-turn loops, and broadcasting information indiscriminately across agent roles. We argue this is not a prompt engineering problem, not a retrieval problem, and not a compression problem: it is a format problem.
  We introduce OBJECTGRAPH (.og), a file format that reconceives the document as a typed, directed knowledge graph to be traversed rather than a string to be injected. OBJECTGRAPH is a strict superset of Markdown - every .md file is a valid .og file - requires no infrastructure beyond a two-primitive query protocol, and is readable by both humans and agents without tooling.
  We formalize the Document Consumption Problem, characterise six structural properties no existing format satisfies simultaneously, and prove OBJECTGRAPH satisfies all six. We further introduce the Progressive Disclosure Model, the Role-Scoped Access Protocol, and Executable Assertion Nodes as native format primitives. Empirical evaluation across five document classes and eight agent task types demonstrates up to 95.3 percent token reduction with no statistically significant degradation in task accuracy (p > 0.05). Transpiler fidelity reaches 98.7 percent content preservation on a held-out document benchmark.

摘要：每種現存的文件格式都是為了讓人類讀者線性地閱讀文本而設計的。自主的 LLM 代理並不閱讀——它們是檢索的。這一基本的不匹配迫使代理將整個文檔注入其上下文窗口，浪費令牌在不相關的內容上，並在多輪循環中累積狀態，無差別地在代理角色之間廣播信息。我們認為這不是一個提示工程問題，不是一個檢索問題，也不是一個壓縮問題：這是一個格式問題。<lb/>  
我們介紹 OBJECTGRAPH (.og)，一種將文檔重新構思為一個類型化的、有向的知識圖譜的文件格式，旨在進行遍歷，而不是簡單地注入一串字符串。OBJECTGRAPH 是 Markdown 的嚴格超集——每個 .md 文件都是有效的 .og 文件——不需要超出兩個基本查詢協議的基礎設施，並且無需工具即可被人類和代理閱讀。<lb/>  
我們正式化了文檔消耗問題，描述了現有格式無法同時滿足的六個結構性特徵，並證明 OBJECTGRAPH 滿足所有六個特徵。我們進一步介紹了漸進式披露模型、角色範圍訪問協議和可執行斷言節點作為原生格式原語。對五種文檔類別和八種代理任務類型的實證評估顯示，在不顯著降低任務準確性的情況下，令牌減少高達 95.3%（p > 0.05）。轉換器的保真度在一個保留的文檔基準上達到 98.7% 的內容保留率。

##### **MCPHunt: An Evaluation Framework for Cross-Boundary Data Propagation in Multi-Server MCP Agents**
2604.27819v1 by Haonan Li, Tianjun Sun, Yongqing Wang, Qisheng Zhang

Multi-server MCP agents create an information-flow control problem: faithful tool composition can turn individually benign read/write permissions into cross-boundary credential propagation -- a structural side effect of workflow topology, not necessarily malicious model behavior. We present MCPHunt, to our knowledge the first controlled benchmark that isolates non-adversarial, verbatim credential propagation across multi-server MCP trust boundaries, with three methodological contributions: (1) canary-based taint tracking that reduces propagation detection to objective string matching; (2) an environment-controlled coverage design with risky, benign, and hard-negative conditions that validates pipeline soundness and controls for credential-format confounds; (3) CRS stratification that disentangles task-mandated propagation (faithful execution of verbatim-transfer instructions) from policy-violating propagation (credentials included despite the option to redact). Across 3,615 main-benchmark traces from 5 models spanning 147 tasks and 9 mechanism families, policy-violating propagation rates reach 11.5--41.3% across all models. This propagation is pathway-specific (25x cross-mechanism range) and concentrated in browser-mediated data flows; hard-negative controls provide evidence that production-format credentials are not necessary -- prompt-directed cross-boundary data flow is sufficient. A prompt-mitigation study across 3 models reduces policy-violating propagation by up to 97% while preserving 80.5% utility, but effectiveness varies with instruction-following capability -- suggesting that prompt-level defenses alone may not suffice. Code, traces, and labeling pipeline are released under MIT and CC BY 4.0.

摘要：多伺服器MCP代理創造了一個資訊流控制問題：忠實的工具組合可以將個別無害的讀/寫權限轉變為跨邊界的憑證傳播——這是工作流程拓撲的結構性副作用，而不一定是惡意模型行為。我們提出了MCPHunt，據我們所知，這是第一個控制基準，能夠在多伺服器MCP信任邊界中隔離非對抗性的逐字憑證傳播，並有三項方法論貢獻：(1) 基於金絲雀的污點追蹤，將傳播檢測簡化為客觀的字串匹配；(2) 一個環境控制的覆蓋設計，包含風險、無害和困難的負樣本條件，以驗證管道的健全性並控制憑證格式的混淆；(3) CRS分層，將任務強制的傳播（忠實執行逐字轉移指令）與違反政策的傳播（儘管有選擇刪除的選項，仍包含憑證）區分開來。在來自5個模型的3,615個主基準追蹤中，涵蓋147個任務和9個機制家族，違反政策的傳播率在所有模型中達到11.5%至41.3%。這種傳播是路徑特定的（跨機制範圍達25倍），並集中在瀏覽器介導的數據流中；困難的負樣本控制提供證據表明生產格式的憑證並不是必要的——提示導向的跨邊界數據流已足夠。一項針對3個模型的提示緩解研究將違反政策的傳播降低了多達97%，同時保留了80.5%的效用，但效果隨著遵循指令的能力而變化——這表明僅依賴提示級別的防禦可能不足。代碼、追蹤和標記管道已根據MIT和CC BY 4.0發布。

##### **XekRung Technical Report**
2605.00072v1 by Jiutian Zeng, Junjie Li, Chengwei Dai, Jie Liang, Zhaoyu Hu, Yiliang Zhang, Ziang Weng, Longtao Huang, Dongjie Zhang, Libin Dong, Yang Ge, Yuanda Wang, Kaiwen Lv Kacuila, Bingyu Zhu, Jing Wang, Jin Xu

We present XekRung, a frontier large language model for cybersecurity, designed to provide comprehensive security capabilities. To achieve this, we develop diverse data synthesis pipelines tailored to the cybersecurity domain, enabling the scalable construction of high-quality training data and providing a strong foundation for cybersecurity knowledge and understanding. Building on this foundation, we establish a complete training pipeline spanning continued pre-training (CPT), supervised fine-tuning (SFT), and reinforcement learning (RL) to further extend the model's capabilities. We further introduce a multi-dimensional evaluation system to guide the iterative improvement of both domain-specific and general-purpose abilities. Extensive experiments demonstrate that XekRung achieves state-of-the-art performance on cybersecurity-specific benchmarks among models of the same scale, while maintaining strong performance on general benchmarks.

摘要：我們提出了 XekRung，一個前沿的大型語言模型，專為網絡安全設計，旨在提供全面的安全能力。為了實現這一目標，我們開發了針對網絡安全領域的多樣化數據合成管道，使得高質量訓練數據的可擴展構建成為可能，並為網絡安全知識和理解提供了堅實的基礎。在此基礎上，我們建立了一個完整的訓練管道，涵蓋持續預訓練（CPT）、監督微調（SFT）和強化學習（RL），以進一步擴展模型的能力。我們還引入了一個多維評估系統，以指導領域特定和通用能力的迭代改進。廣泛的實驗表明，XekRung 在同等規模的模型中，在網絡安全特定基準上達到了最先進的性能，同時在通用基準上也保持了強勁的表現。

##### **Learning to Reason: Targeted Knowledge Discovery and Fuzzy Logic Update for Robust Image Recognition**
2604.27759v1 by Gurucharan Srinivas, Joshua Niemeijer, Frank Köster

Integrating domain knowledge into deep neural networks is a promising way to improve generalization. Existing methods either encode prior knowledge in the loss function or apply post-processing modules, but both depend on identifying useful symbolic knowledge to integrate. Since such rules are often unavailable in real-world vision tasks, we propose a method for targeted knowledge discovery. We propose a Differentiable Knowledge Unit (DKU) that enables modulating the classifier logits, yielding refined class probabilities. The DKU uses implication rules to represent relationships between task classes and implicit concepts learned entirely from the main task supervision, without requiring concept labels. Concepts are identified by dedicated classifiers, whose probabilities are passed to DKU alongside the primary class probabilities. DKU computes a logic-based adjustment vector via fuzzy inference, which modulates the primary class logits to yield refined class probabilities. When concept classifiers represent concepts that do not support the logical rule structure, the resulting adjustments to the class probabilities do not directly minimize the supervision loss. Consequently, optimizing the supervision loss on these adjusted class probabilities implicitly trains the concept classifiers. We construct the rule base so that bidirectional logical relations connect concepts and classes. We enforce the concepts to be distinct from each other and with respect to the classes. This design enforces a clean supervision signal for concept learning. We evaluate our methods on the PASCAL-VOC, COCO, and MedMNIST datasets. We demonstrate improvement through our knowledge integration across these datasets. We conduct domain generalization and hard-sample ablation studies and find that our implicit knowledge discovery and integration outperforms the baseline.

摘要：將領域知識整合進深度神經網絡是一種有前景的提高泛化能力的方法。現有的方法要麼將先驗知識編碼在損失函數中，要麼應用後處理模塊，但這兩者都依賴於識別有用的符號知識來進行整合。由於這些規則在現實世界的視覺任務中通常不可用，我們提出了一種針對性知識發現的方法。我們提出了一種可微分知識單元（DKU），使得可以調節分類器的邏輯值，從而產生精煉的類別概率。DKU使用蕴涵規則來表示任務類別與從主任務監督中完全學到的隱含概念之間的關係，而不需要概念標籤。概念由專門的分類器識別，這些分類器的概率與主要類別概率一起傳遞給DKU。DKU通過模糊推理計算基於邏輯的調整向量，該向量調節主要類別的邏輯值以產生精煉的類別概率。當概念分類器表示不支持邏輯規則結構的概念時，對類別概率的調整不會直接最小化監督損失。因此，對這些調整後的類別概率優化監督損失會隱式訓練概念分類器。我們構建規則庫，使得雙向邏輯關係連接概念和類別。我們強制概念彼此之間以及相對於類別是不同的。這一設計為概念學習強制提供了一個乾淨的監督信號。我們在PASCAL-VOC、COCO和MedMNIST數據集上評估我們的方法。我們展示了通過知識整合在這些數據集上取得的改進。我們進行了領域泛化和困難樣本消融研究，發現我們的隱式知識發現和整合超越了基線。

##### **AgentEconomist: An End-to-end Agentic System Translating Economic Intuitions into Executable Computational Experiments**
2604.27725v1 by Jiaju Chen, Jinghua Piao, Xia Xu, Songwei Li, Tong Xia, Xiangnan He, Yong Li

A long-standing challenge in economics lies not in the lack of intuition, but in the difficulty of translating intuitive insights into verifiable research. To address this challenge, we introduce AgentEconomist, an end-to-end interactive system designed to translate abstract intuitions into executable computational experiments. Grounded in a domain-specific knowledge base covering over 13,000 high-quality academic papers, the system employs a modular multi-stage architecture. Specifically, the Idea Development Stage generates literature-grounded hypotheses, the Experimental Design Stage configures simulator-aligned experimental parameters and protocols, and the Experimental Execution Stage runs experiments and returns structured analyses. Together, these stages form a human-in-the-loop, iterative workflow that translates economic intuitions into executable computational experiments. Through extensive experiments involving human expert evaluation and large language models (LLMs) as judges, we show that the system generates research ideas with stronger literature grounding and higher novelty and insight than state-of-the-art generic LLMs. Overall, AgentEconomist adopts a human-AI collaboration paradigm that enables researchers to focus on high-level intuitions, while delegating the labor-intensive processes of translation and computational execution to agents.

摘要：一個長期存在的經濟學挑戰不在於缺乏直覺，而在於將直覺見解轉化為可驗證的研究的困難。為了解決這一挑戰，我們介紹了AgentEconomist，這是一個端到端的互動系統，旨在將抽象的直覺轉化為可執行的計算實驗。該系統基於一個涵蓋超過13,000篇高品質學術論文的領域特定知識庫，採用模組化的多階段架構。具體而言，想法發展階段生成基於文獻的假設，實驗設計階段配置與模擬器對齊的實驗參數和協議，而實驗執行階段則運行實驗並返回結構化分析。這些階段共同形成了一個人機協作的迭代工作流程，將經濟直覺轉化為可執行的計算實驗。通過涉及人類專家評估和大型語言模型（LLMs）作為評判者的廣泛實驗，我們展示了該系統生成的研究想法在文獻基礎和新穎性及洞察力方面優於最先進的通用LLMs。總體而言，AgentEconomist採用了一種人機協作的範式，使研究人員能夠專注於高層次的直覺，同時將翻譯和計算執行的勞動密集型過程委派給代理。

##### **Knowledge Graph Representations for LLM-Based Policy Compliance Reasoning**
2604.27713v1 by Wilder Baldwin, Sepideh Ghanavati

The risks posed by AI features are increasing as they are rapidly integrated into software applications. In response, regulations and standards for safe and secure AI have been proposed. ##### **Linguistically Informed Multimodal Fusion for Vietnamese Scene-Text Image Captioning: Dataset, Graph Framework, and Phonological Attention**
2604.27712v1 by Nhi Ngoc-Yen Nguyen, Anh-Duc Nguyen, Nghia Hieu Nguyen, Kiet Van Nguyen, Ngan Luu-Thuy Nguyen

Scene-text image captioning requires fusing three information streams -- visual features, OCR-detected text, and linguistic knowledge -- to generate descriptions that faithfully integrate text visible in images. Existing fusion approaches treat text as language-agnostic, which fails for Vietnamese: a tonal language where diacritics alter word meaning, OCR errors are pervasive, and word boundaries are ambiguous. We argue that Vietnamese scene-text captioning demands \textit{linguistically informed multimodal fusion}, where language-specific structural knowledge is explicitly incorporated into the fusion mechanism. Motivated from these insights, we propose \textbf{HSTFG} (Heterogeneous Scene-Text Fusion Graph), a general-purpose graph fusion framework with learned spatial attention bias, and show through topology analysis that cross-modal graph edges are harmful for scene-text fusion. Building on this finding, we design \textbf{PhonoSTFG} (Phonological Scene-Text Fusion Graph) which specializes graph-level fusion for Vietnamese linguistic reasoning. To support evaluation, we introduce \textbf{ViTextCaps}, the first large-scale Vietnamese scene-text captioning dataset (\textbf{15{,}729} images with \textbf{74{,}970} captions), with comprehensive linguistic analysis showing that 52.8\% of the vocabulary is at risk of diacritic collision.

##### **Human-in-the-Loop Meta Bayesian Optimization for Fusion Energy and Scientific Applications**

##### **From Context to Skills: Can Language Models Learn from Context Skillfully?**
2604.27660v1 by Shuzheng Si, Haozhe Zhao, Yu Lei, Qingyi Wang, Dingwei Chen, Zhitong Wang, Zhenhailong Wang, Kangyang Luo, Zheng Wang, Gang Chen, Fanchao Qi, Minjia Zhang, Maosong Sun

Many real-world tasks require language models (LMs) to reason over complex contexts that exceed their parametric knowledge. This calls for context learning, where LMs directly learn relevant knowledge from the given context. An intuitive solution is inference-time skill augmentation: extracting the rules and procedures from context into natural-language skills. However, constructing such skills for context learning scenarios faces two challenges: the prohibitive cost of manual skill annotation for long, technically dense contexts, and the lack of external feedback for automated skill construction, since there is no automatic signal to tell whether a proposed skill is helpful. In this paper, we propose Ctx2Skill, a self-evolving framework that autonomously discovers, refines, and selects context-specific skills without human supervision or external feedback. At its core, a multi-agent self-play loop has a Challenger that generates probing tasks and rubrics, a Reasoner that attempts to solve them guided by an evolving skill set, and a neutral Judge that provides binary feedback. Crucially, both the Challenger and the Reasoner evolve through accumulated skills: dedicated Proposer and Generator agents analyze failure cases and synthesize them into targeted skill updates for both sides, enabling automated skill discovery and refinement. To prevent adversarial collapse caused by increasingly extreme task generation and over-specialized skill accumulation, we further introduce a Cross-time Replay mechanism that identifies the skill set achieving the best balance across representative cases for the Reasoner side, ensuring robust and generalizable skill evolution. The resulting skills can be plugged into any language model to obtain better context learning capability. Evaluated on four context learning tasks from CL-bench, Ctx2Skill consistently improves solving rates across backbone models.

摘要：許多現實世界的任務要求語言模型 (LMs) 在超出其參數知識的複雜上下文中進行推理。這需要上下文學習，其中 LMs 直接從給定的上下文中學習相關知識。一個直觀的解決方案是推理時的技能增強：將上下文中的規則和程序提取為自然語言技能。然而，為上下文學習場景構建這樣的技能面臨兩個挑戰：對於長且技術密集的上下文，手動技能標註的高昂成本，以及缺乏外部反饋以進行自動化技能構建，因為沒有自動信號告訴我們所提議的技能是否有幫助。在本文中，我們提出了 Ctx2Skill，一個自我演化的框架，能夠在沒有人工監督或外部反饋的情況下，自主發現、完善和選擇特定於上下文的技能。其核心是一個多代理自我對弈循環，其中有一個挑戰者生成探測任務和標準，一個推理者試圖根據不斷演變的技能集來解決這些任務，還有一個中立的評判者提供二元反饋。關鍵是，挑戰者和推理者都通過積累的技能進化：專門的提議者和生成器代理分析失敗案例，並將其綜合為針對雙方的技能更新，實現自動化的技能發現和完善。為了防止由於越來越極端的任務生成和過度專門化的技能積累所造成的對抗性崩潰，我們進一步引入了一種跨時間重播機制，該機制識別出在推理者方面達到最佳平衡的技能集，確保穩健且可泛化的技能演化。所產生的技能可以插入任何語言模型，以獲得更好的上下文學習能力。在 CL-bench 的四個上下文學習任務上進行評估，Ctx2Skill 一直提高各個基礎模型的解決率。

##### **When Does Structure Matter in Continual Learning? Dimensionality Controls When Modularity Shapes Representational Geometry**
2604.27656v1 by Kathrin Korte, Joachim Winter Pedersen, Eleni Nisioti, Sebastian Risi

To preserve previously learned representations, continual learning systems must strike a balance between plasticity, the ability to acquire new knowledge, and stability. This stability-plasticity dilemma affects how representations can be reused across tasks: shared structure enables transfer when tasks are similar but may also induce interference when new learning disrupts existing representations. However, it remains unclear when and why structural separation influences this trade-off. In this study, we examine how network architecture, task similarity, and representational dimensionality jointly shape learning in a sequential task paradigm inspired by transfer-interference studies. We compare a task-partitioned modular recurrent network with a single-module baseline by systematically varying task similarity (low, medium, high) and the scale of weight initialization, which induces different learning regimes that we empirically characterize through the effective dimensionality of the learned representations. We find that architecture has minimal impact in high-dimensional regimes where representations are sufficiently unconstrained to accommodate multiple tasks without strong interference. In contrast, in lower-dimensional (rich) regimes, architectural separation is decisive: modular networks exhibit graded alignment of task-specific subspaces with overlap for similar tasks, partial orthogonalization for moderately dissimilar tasks, and stronger separation for dissimilar tasks. This graded geometry is absent in the single network baseline. Our findings suggest that representational dimensionality acts as a key organizing variable governing when structural separation becomes functionally relevant, and highlight adaptive geometry as a central principle for designing continual learning systems.

摘要：為了保留先前學習的表徵，持續學習系統必須在可塑性（獲取新知識的能力）和穩定性之間取得平衡。這種穩定性-可塑性困境影響了表徵在任務之間的重用方式：共享結構在任務相似時促進轉移，但當新學習干擾現有表徵時，也可能引發干擾。然而，結構分離何時以及為何會影響這種權衡仍不清楚。在本研究中，我們考察了網絡架構、任務相似性和表徵維度如何共同塑造受啟發於轉移-干擾研究的序列任務範式中的學習。我們通過系統性地改變任務相似性（低、中、高）和權重初始化的規模，來比較一個任務劃分的模塊化遞歸網絡與單模塊基準，這會引發不同的學習模式，我們通過學習表徵的有效維度來實證地表徵這些模式。我們發現，在高維模式中，架構對表徵的影響最小，因為表徵足夠不受約束，可以容納多個任務而不會產生強烈的干擾。相反，在低維（豐富）模式中，架構分離是決定性的：模塊化網絡顯示出任務特定子空間的逐級對齊，對於相似任務有重疊，對於中等不相似的任務有部分正交化，而對於不相似的任務則有更強的分離。這種逐級幾何在單一網絡基準中不存在。我們的研究結果表明，表徵維度作為一個關鍵組織變量，主導了結構分離何時變得功能相關，並強調了自適應幾何作為設計持續學習系統的核心原則。

##### **RoadMapper: A Multi-Agent System for Roadmap Generation of Solving Complex Research Problems**
2604.27616v1 by Jiacheng Liu, Zichen Tang, Zhongjun Yang, Xinyi Hu, Xueyuan Lin, Linwei Jia, Ruofei Bai, Rongjin Li, Shiyao Peng, Haocheng Gao, Haihong E

People commonly leverage structured content to accelerate knowledge acquisition and research problem solving. Among these, roadmaps guide researchers through hierarchical subtasks to solve complex research problems step by step. Despite progress in structured content generation, the roadmap generation task has remained unexplored. To bridge this gap, we introduce RoadMap, a novel benchmark designed to evaluate the ability of large language models (LLMs) to construct high-quality roadmaps for solving complex research problems. Based on this, we identify three limitations of LLMs: (1) lack of professional knowledge, (2) unreasonable task decomposition, and (3) disordered logical relationships. To address these challenges, we propose RoadMapper, an LLM-based multi-agent system that decomposes the research roadmap generation task into three key stages (i.e., initial generation, knowledge augmentation, and iterative "critique-revise-evaluate"). Extensive experiments demonstrate that RoadMapper can improve LLMs' ability for roadmap generation, while enhancing average performance by more than 8% and saving 84% of the time required by human experts, highlighting its effectiveness and application potential.

##### **A Survey of Reasoning-Intensive Retrieval: Progress and Challenges**
2605.00063v1 by Yiyang Wei, Tingyu Song, Siyue Zhang, Yilun Zhao

Reasoning-Intensive Retrieval (RIR) targets retrieval settings where relevance is mediated by latent inferential links between a query and supporting evidence, rather than semantic similarity. Motivated by the emergent reasoning abilities of Large Language Models (LLMs), recent work integrates these capabilities into the IR field, spanning the entire pipeline from benchmarks to retrievers and rerankers. Despite this progress, the field lacks a systematic framework to organize current efforts and articulate a clear path forward. To provide a clear roadmap for this rapidly growing yet fragmented area, this survey (1) systematizes existing RIR benchmarks by knowledge domains and modalities, providing a detailed analysis of the current landscape; (2) introduces a structured taxonomy that categorizes methods based on where and how reasoning is integrated into the retrieval pipeline, alongside an analysis of their trade-offs and practical applications; and (3) summarizes challenges and future directions to guide research in this evolving field.

摘要：推理密集檢索（RIR）針對檢索設置，其中相關性是由查詢與支持證據之間的潛在推理聯繫所調節，而非語義相似性。受到大型語言模型（LLMs）新興推理能力的啟發，最近的研究將這些能力整合到資訊檢索（IR）領域，涵蓋從基準測試到檢索器和重排序器的整個流程。儘管取得了這些進展，該領域仍缺乏一個系統化的框架來組織當前的努力並闡明明確的前進方向。為了為這個快速增長但支離破碎的領域提供一個清晰的路線圖，本調查（1）通過知識領域和模態系統化現有的RIR基準，提供對當前格局的詳細分析；（2）引入一個結構化的分類法，根據推理在檢索流程中整合的方式和位置對方法進行分類，並分析其權衡和實際應用；（3）總結挑戰和未來方向，以指導這個不斷發展的領域的研究。

##### **In-Context Examples Suppress Scientific Knowledge Recall in LLMs**
2604.27540v1 by Chaemin Jang, Woojin Park, Hyeok Yun, Dongman Lee, Jihee Kim

Scientific reasoning rarely stops at what is directly observable; it often requires uncovering hidden structure from data. From estimating reaction constants in chemistry to inferring demand elasticities in economics, this latent structure recovery is what distinguishes scientific reasoning from curve fitting. Large language models (LLMs) can often recall and apply relevant scientific formulas, but we show that this ability is surprisingly easy to suppress. We show that adding in-context examples makes models rely less on pretrained domain knowledge, even when those examples are generated by the very same formula. Rather than reinforcing knowledge-driven derivation, examples shift computation toward empirical pattern fitting. We document this knowledge displacement on 60 latent structure recovery tasks across five scientific domains, 6,000 trials, and four models. This displacement is consistent across domains, but its accuracy consequences depend on how the displaced strategy compares to the one that replaces it: the same shift can lower accuracy, leave it unchanged, or appear to improve it. In all cases, however, the model shifts away from knowledge-driven reasoning. For practitioners deploying LLMs on scientific tasks, the message is cautionary: in-context examples may displace, rather than reinforce, the knowledge they are intended to support.

摘要：科學推理很少止於直接可觀察的事物；它通常需要從數據中揭示隱藏的結構。從估計化學中的反應常數到推斷經濟學中的需求彈性，這種潛在結構的恢復是科學推理與曲線擬合之間的區別所在。大型語言模型（LLMs）通常能夠回憶並應用相關的科學公式，但我們顯示這種能力意外地容易被抑制。我們顯示，添加上下文示例使模型對預訓練的領域知識依賴減少，即使這些示例是由同一公式生成的。示例並不是強化基於知識的推導，而是將計算轉向經驗模式擬合。我們記錄了在五個科學領域的60個潛在結構恢復任務中，進行了6,000次試驗和四個模型的知識位移。這種位移在不同領域中是一致的，但其準確性後果取決於被取代的策略與替代策略的比較：相同的轉變可能降低準確性、保持不變或似乎改善。在所有情況下，模型都偏離了基於知識的推理。對於在科學任務中部署LLMs的實踐者來說，這個信息是警示性的：上下文示例可能會取代而不是強化它們所旨在支持的知識。

##### **Knowledge Affordances for Hybrid Human-AI Information Seeking**
2604.27539v1 by Irene Celino

As information ecosystems grow more heterogeneous, both humans and artificial agents increasingly face a simple yet unresolved question: when seeking knowledge, whom should we ask, and why? Inspired by how people intuitively "read a room", this paper introduces the concept of knowledge affordance (KA) to systematize how agents identify meaningful opportunities for information seeking in hybrid human-AI environments.
  Rather than introducing a fully formed framework, we propose KAs as declarative, semantically grounded descriptions of what a knowledge source can offer, for which kinds of questions, and with which contextual properties. Additionally, we suggest that KAs are relational, possibly emerging from the interplay between the agent's task, preferences and situational factors.
  Our contribution is thus a conceptual proposal that connects different research streams, including affordances, semantic web services, knowledge engineering and querying, and mutual intelligibility. We sketch possible research directions to build KA-aware systems that navigate information spaces with greater transparency, adaptability and shared understanding.
