##### **Improving Graph Few-shot Learning with Hyperbolic Space and Denoising Diffusion**
2604.27462v1 by Yonghao Liu, Jialu Sun, Wei Pang, Fausto Giunchiglia, Ximing Li, Xiaoyue Feng, Renchu Guan

Graph few-shot learning, which focuses on effectively learning from only a small number of labeled nodes to quickly adapt to new tasks, has garnered significant research attention. Despite recent advances in graph few-shot learning that have demonstrated promising performance, existing methods still suffer from several key limitations. First, during the meta-training phase, these methods typically perform node representation learning in Euclidean space, which often fails to capture the inherently hierarchical structure existing in real-world graph data. Second, during the meta-testing phase, they usually fit an empirical target distribution derived from only a few support samples, even when this distribution significantly deviates from the true underlying distribution. To address these issues, we propose IMPRESS, a novel framework that IMproves graPh few-shot learning with hypeRbolic spacE and denoiSing diffuSion. Specifically, our model learns node representations in a hyperbolic space and enriches the support distribution through denoising diffusion mechanisms. Theoretically, IMPRESS achieves a tighter generalization bound. Empirically, IMPRESS consistently outperforms competitive baselines across multiple benchmark datasets.

摘要：圖形少樣本學習專注於僅從少量標記節點中有效學習，以快速適應新任務，已引起了顯著的研究關注。儘管最近在圖形少樣本學習方面的進展顯示出有前景的表現，但現有方法仍然存在幾個主要限制。首先，在元訓練階段，這些方法通常在歐幾里得空間中執行節點表示學習，這往往無法捕捉現實世界圖形數據中固有的層次結構。其次，在元測試階段，它們通常僅從少數支持樣本中擬合一個實證目標分佈，即使這個分佈與真實的潛在分佈有顯著偏差。為了解決這些問題，我們提出了IMPRESS，一個新穎的框架，通過超曲面空間和去噪擴散來改善圖形少樣本學習。具體而言，我們的模型在超曲面空間中學習節點表示，並通過去噪擴散機制豐富支持分佈。在理論上，IMPRESS實現了更緊的泛化界限。在實證上，IMPRESS在多個基準數據集上始終超越競爭基準。

##### **From Unstructured to Structured: LLM-Guided Attribute Graphs for Entity Search and Ranking**
2604.27410v1 by Yilun Zhu, Nikhita Vedula, Shervin Malmasi

Entity search, i.e., finding the most similar entities to a query entity, faces unique challenges in e-commerce, where product similarity varies across categories and contexts. Traditional embedding-based approaches often struggle to capture nuanced context-specific attribute relevance. In this paper, we present a two-stage approach combining Large Language Model (LLM)-driven attribute graph construction with graph-aware LLM ranking. In the offline stage, we extract structured product attributes from unstructured text, and construct a reusable attribute graph with category-aware schemas. ##### **Robust Learning on Heterogeneous Graphs with Heterophily: A Graph Structure Learning Approach**
2604.27387v1 by Yihan Zhang, Ercan E. Kuruoglu

Heterogeneous graphs with heterophily have emerged as a powerful abstraction for modeling complex real-world systems, where nodes of different types and labels interact in diverse and often non-homophilous ways. Despite recent advances, robust representation learning for such graphs remains largely unexplored, particularly in the presence of noisy or misleading connectivity. In this work, we investigate this problem and identify structural noise as a critical challenge that significantly degrades model performance. To address this issue, we propose a unified framework, Heterogeneous Graph Unified Learning (HGUL), which jointly handles heterophily and noisy graph structures. The framework consists of three complementary modules: a kNN-based graph construction module that recovers reliable local neighborhoods, a graph structure learning module that adaptively refines the adjacency by filtering noisy edges, and a heterogeneous affinity learning module that captures class-level relationships via an extended affinity matrix derived from a polynomial graph kernel. Extensive experiments on multiple datasets demonstrate that HGUL consistently outperforms existing methods on clean graphs and maintains strong robustness under varying levels of structural noise. The results further underscore the importance of jointly modeling heterophily and noise in heterogeneous graph learning.

##### **TypeBandit: Type-Level Context Allocation and Reweighting for Effective Attribute Completion in Heterogeneous Graph Neural Networks**
2604.27356v1 by Ta-Yang Wang, Rajgopal Kannan, Viktor Prasanna

Heterogeneous graphs are widely used to model multi-relational systems, but missing node attributes remain a major bottleneck for downstream learning. In this paper, we identify and formalize type-dependent information asymmetry: the phenomenon that different node types provide substantially different levels of useful signal for attribute completion. Motivated by this observation, we propose TypeBandit, a lightweight, model-agnostic methodology for heterogeneous attribute completion. TypeBandit combines topology-aware initialization, type-level bandit sampling, and joint representation learning. It allocates a finite global sampling budget across node types, samples representative nodes within each type, and uses the resulting sampled type summaries as shared contextual signals during representation construction. By operating at the type level rather than over each target node's local neighborhood, TypeBandit keeps the adaptive state compact and practical for large heterogeneous graphs.
  A key advantage of TypeBandit is architectural flexibility. Rather than requiring a new heterogeneous graph neural network architecture, TypeBandit acts as a type-aware front end for representative heterogeneous GNN backbones, including R-GCN, HetGNN, HGT, and SimpleHGN. We further introduce a hybrid pretraining scheme that combines structural degree priors with feature propagation, yielding a more reliable initializer than degree-only pretraining. Under a fixed-split protocol on DBLP, IMDB, and ACM, TypeBandit provides dataset-dependent but practically meaningful gains. Additional ablation, stability, efficiency, semantic-propagation, and sampled OGBN-MAG experiments support TypeBandit as a practical strategy for heterogeneous attribute completion when type-specific information is unevenly distributed and sampling resources are limited.

摘要：異質圖廣泛用於建模多關係系統，但缺失的節點屬性仍然是下游學習的主要瓶頸。在本文中，我們識別並形式化了類型依賴的信息不對稱：不同節點類型提供的有用信號在屬性補全方面存在實質性差異的現象。基於這一觀察，我們提出了TypeBandit，一種輕量級、模型無關的異質屬性補全方法。TypeBandit結合了拓撲感知初始化、類型級別的賭徒抽樣和聯合表示學習。它在節點類型之間分配有限的全局抽樣預算，在每種類型內抽樣代表性節點，並在表示構建過程中使用所得到的抽樣類型摘要作為共享的上下文信號。通過在類型級別運作，而不是針對每個目標節點的局部鄰域，TypeBandit保持了自適應狀態的緊湊性，並且對於大型異質圖是實用的。

TypeBandit的一個主要優勢是架構靈活性。TypeBandit不需要新的異質圖神經網絡架構，而是作為代表性異質GNN骨幹的類型感知前端，包括R-GCN、HetGNN、HGT和SimpleHGN。我們進一步引入了一種混合預訓練方案，將結構度先驗與特徵傳播相結合，從而產生比僅基於度的預訓練更可靠的初始化器。在DBLP、IMDB和ACM的固定劃分協議下，TypeBandit提供了依賴於數據集但在實際上有意義的增益。額外的消融、穩定性、效率、語義傳播和抽樣OGBN-MAG實驗支持TypeBandit作為一種實用的異質屬性補全策略，特別是在類型特定信息不均勻分佈且抽樣資源有限的情況下。

##### **BoostLoRA: Growing Effective Rank by Boosting Adapters**
2604.27308v1 by Raviteja Anantha, Nick Levato, Layne C. Price

Parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) methods face a tradeoff between adapter size and expressivity: ultra-low-parameter adapters are confined to fixed low-rank subspaces, capping performance even with extended training. We propose BoostLoRA, a gradient-boosting framework that overcomes this limit by iteratively training and merging minimal adapters on the examples the current model gets wrong. A ROTATE SVD basis strategy assigns each round to an orthogonal subspace, so cumulative effective rank grows linearly with the number of rounds while each adapter remains ultra-low-rank. After merging, adapters are discarded, leaving zero inference overhead. On Qwen2.5-3B, BoostLoRA reaches 89.1% on GSM8K and 68.8% on MATH-500, surpassing both the best single-shot ultra-low parameter adapter (TinyLoRA) and full fine-tuning; on code generation it reaches 57.2% on MBPP and 80.4% on HumanEval while full fine-tuning drops below the zero-shot baseline. We also demonstrate cross-architecture transfer on protein binding classification with ESM2-650M and cross-entropy training. BoostLoRA is, to our knowledge, the first PEFT method whose effective rank grows with training, separating per-round parameter cost from total representational capacity.

摘要：參數高效微調（PEFT）方法面臨適配器大小和表達能力之間的權衡：超低參數適配器被限制在固定的低秩子空間中，即使在擴展訓練下也無法提高性能。我們提出了BoostLoRA，一種通過迭代訓練和合併最小適配器來克服這一限制的梯度提升框架，針對當前模型錯誤的例子進行操作。一種ROTATE SVD基礎策略將每一輪分配給一個正交子空間，因此累積有效秩隨著輪次的增加而線性增長，同時每個適配器保持超低秩。在合併後，適配器被丟棄，沒有額外的推理開銷。在Qwen2.5-3B上，BoostLoRA在GSM8K上達到89.1%，在MATH-500上達到68.8%，超越了最佳單次超低參數適配器（TinyLoRA）和完整微調；在代碼生成方面，它在MBPP上達到57.2%，在HumanEval上達到80.4%，而完整微調則低於零-shot基線。我們還展示了在蛋白質結合分類中使用ESM2-650M和交叉熵訓練的跨架構轉移。據我們所知，BoostLoRA是第一個隨著訓練而增長有效秩的PEFT方法，將每輪的參數成本與總表現能力分開。

##### **Machine Collective Intelligence for Explainable Scientific Discovery**
2604.27297v1 by Gyoung S. Na, Chanyoung Park

Deriving governing equations from empirical observations is a longstanding challenge in science. Although artificial intelligence (AI) has demonstrated substantial capabilities in function approximation, the discovery of explainable and extrapolatable equations remains a fundamental limitation of modern AI, posing a central bottleneck for AI-driven scientific discovery. Here, we present machine collective intelligence, a unified paradigm that integrates two fundamental yet distinct traditions in computational intelligence--symbolism and metaheuristics--to enable autonomous and evolutionary discovery of governing equations. It orchestrates multiple reasoning agents to evolve their symbolic hypotheses through coordinated generation, evaluation, critique, and consolidation, enabling scientific discovery beyond single-agent inference. Across scientific systems governed by deterministic, stochastic, or previously uncharacterized dynamics, machine collective intelligence autonomously recovered the underlying governing equations without relying on hand-crafted domain knowledge. Furthermore, the resulting equations reduced extrapolation error by up to six orders of magnitude relative to deep neural networks, while condensing 0.5-1 million model parameters into just 5-40 interpretable parameters. This study marks an important shift in AI toward the autonomous discovery of principled scientific equations.

摘要：從經驗觀察中推導出治理方程式一直是科學中的一項長期挑戰。儘管人工智慧（AI）在函數近似方面展現了相當的能力，但可解釋和可外推方程式的發現仍然是現代AI的一個基本限制，對AI驅動的科學發現構成了核心瓶頸。在這裡，我們提出了機器集體智慧，這是一種統一的範式，整合了計算智能中的兩種基本但不同的傳統——符號學和元啟發式方法——以實現治理方程式的自主和進化發現。它協調多個推理代理，通過協同生成、評估、批評和整合來進化其符號假設，使得科學發現超越單一代理的推斷。在由確定性、隨機性或先前未特徵化的動力學所主導的科學系統中，機器集體智慧自主恢復了潛在的治理方程式，而無需依賴手工製作的領域知識。此外，所得到的方程式相對於深度神經網絡將外推誤差降低了多達六個數量級，同時將50萬到100萬個模型參數壓縮為僅5到40個可解釋的參數。本研究標誌著AI在自主發現原則性科學方程式方面的重要轉變。

##### **Learning Rate Engineering: From Coarse Single Parameter to Layered Evolution**
2604.27295v1 by Ming-Hong Yao, Di Wang, Jian Cui, Jin-Yan Chen, Zi-Hao Cui, Fa Wang, Chen Wei, Qiu-Ye Yu

Learning rate scheduling has evolved from the single global fixed rate of early SGD to sophisticated layer-wise adaptive strategies. We systematize this evolution into five generations: (Gen1) global fixed learning rates, (Gen2) global scheduling, (Gen3) parameter-level adaptation, (Gen4) layer-level differentiation, and (Gen5) joint layer-time scheduling. We trace the fundamental motivation behind each transition, showing how the shift from one-size-fits-all to tailoring by layer and time addresses the impossible trinity of transfer learning: lower layers require small updates to preserve general knowledge while higher layers need large updates to adapt to new tasks. Building on this taxonomy, we propose Discriminative Adaptive Layer Scaling (DALS), a unified framework that integrates phase-adaptive cosine scheduling, depth-aware Grokfast gradient filtering, and LARS-style trust ratios into a single coherent optimizer. We benchmark 18 strategies including three DALS variants across all five generations on five datasets: synthetic, CIFAR-10 (from scratch), RTE, TREC-6, and IMDb (fine-tuning). On synthetic, DALS achieves the best accuracy at 98.0%, while DALS-Fast reaches 90% in just 3 epochs. The cross-dataset analysis reveals striking regime-dependent patterns -- no single strategy wins across all regimes. Critically, STLR+Discriminative, the ULMFiT champion, catastrophically fails on from-scratch tasks (43.6% on TREC-6 from scratch vs. 96.8% with RAdam), confirming that directional decay biases are harmful without pretrained features. DALS avoids either extreme, achieving the best synthetic result while maintaining competitive fine-tuning performance.

摘要：學習率調度已從早期SGD的單一全局固定率演變為複雜的層級自適應策略。<lb/>我們將這一演變系統化為五個世代： (Gen1) 全球固定學習率， (Gen2) 全球調度， (Gen3) 參數級別適應， (Gen4) 層級差異化，以及 (Gen5) 聯合層時間調度。<lb/>我們追溯每次轉變背後的基本動機，顯示從一刀切到按層和時間量身定制的轉變如何解決轉移學習的三難困境：較低層需要小的更新以保持一般知識，而較高層則需要大的更新以適應新任務。<lb/>基於這一分類法，我們提出了判別自適應層縮放（DALS），這是一個統一框架，將階段自適應餘弦調度、深度感知Grokfast梯度過濾和LARS風格的信任比率整合為一個一致的優化器。<lb/>我們在五個數據集上基準測試了18種策略，包括三種DALS變體，這五個數據集分別是：合成數據、CIFAR-10（從頭開始）、RTE、TREC-6和IMDb（微調）。<lb/>在合成數據上，DALS達到了98.0%的最佳準確率，而DALS-Fast在僅僅3個時期內達到了90%。<lb/>跨數據集分析揭示了驚人的制度依賴模式——沒有單一策略在所有制度中獲勝。<lb/>關鍵是，STLR+Discriminative，ULMFiT的冠軍，在從頭開始的任務上慘遭失敗（TREC-6從頭開始的準確率為43.6%，而使用RAdam則為96.8%），確認了方向性衰減偏差在沒有預訓練特徵的情況下是有害的。<lb/>DALS避免了任何極端，在保持競爭性微調性能的同時，實現了最佳的合成結果。

##### **Learning When to Remember: Risk-Sensitive Contextual Bandits for Abstention-Aware Memory Retrieval in LLM-Based Coding Agents**
2604.27283v1 by Mehmet Iscan

Large language model (LLM)-based coding agents increasingly rely on external memory to reuse prior debugging experience, repair traces, and repository-local operational knowledge. However, retrieved memory is useful only when the current failure is genuinely compatible with a previous one; superficial similarity in stack traces, terminal errors, paths, or configuration symptoms can lead to unsafe memory injection. This paper reframes issue-memory use as a selective, risk-sensitive control problem rather than a pure top-k retrieval problem. We introduce RSCB-MC, a risk-sensitive contextual bandit memory controller that decides whether an agent should use no memory, inject the top resolution, summarize multiple candidates, perform high-precision or high-recall retrieval, abstain, or ask for feedback. The system stores reusable issue knowledge through a pattern-variant-episode schema and converts retrieval evidence into a fixed 16-feature contextual state capturing relevance, uncertainty, structural compatibility, feedback history, false-positive risk, latency, and token cost. Its reward design penalizes false-positive memory injection more strongly than missed reuse, making non-injection and abstention first-class safety actions. In deterministic smoke-scale artifacts, RSCB-MC obtains the strongest non-oracle offline replay success rate, 62.5%, while maintaining a 0.0% false-positive rate. In a bounded 200-case hot-path validation, it reaches 60.5% proxy success with 0.0% false positives and a 331.466 microseconds p95 decision latency. The results show that, for coding-agent memory, the key question is not only which memory is most similar, but whether any retrieved memory is safe enough to influence the debugging trajectory.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLM）基礎的編碼代理越來越依賴外部記憶來重用先前的除錯經驗、修復痕跡和庫本地的操作知識。<lb/>然而，檢索到的記憶僅在當前的失敗與先前的失敗真正相容時才有用；堆疊追蹤、終端錯誤、路徑或配置症狀的表面相似性可能導致不安全的記憶注入。<lb/>本文將問題記憶的使用重新框架為一個選擇性、風險敏感的控制問題，而不是純粹的 top-k 檢索問題。<lb/>我們介紹了 RSCB-MC，一種風險敏感的上下文強盜記憶控制器，它決定代理是否應該不使用記憶、注入最佳解決方案、總結多個候選方案、執行高精度或高召回檢索、放棄或請求反饋。<lb/>該系統通過模式變體事件架構存儲可重用的問題知識，並將檢索證據轉換為固定的 16 特徵上下文狀態，以捕捉相關性、不確定性、結構相容性、反饋歷史、假陽性風險、延遲和標記成本。<lb/>其獎勵設計對假陽性記憶注入的懲罰比錯過重用更強，讓不注入和放棄成為一級安全行動。<lb/>在確定性煙霧規模的工件中，RSCB-MC 獲得了最強的非神諭離線重播成功率 62.5%，同時保持 0.0% 的假陽性率。<lb/>在一個有界的 200 案例熱路驗證中，它達到了 60.5% 的代理成功率，假陽性為 0.0%，決策延遲為 331.466 微秒的 p95。<lb/>結果顯示，對於編碼代理記憶，關鍵問題不僅是哪些記憶最相似，而是任何檢索到的記憶是否足夠安全以影響除錯軌跡。

##### **OptimusKG: Unifying biomedical knowledge in a modern multimodal graph**
2604.27269v1 by Lucas Vittor, Ayush Noori, Iñaki Arango, Joaquín Polonuer, Sam Rodriques, Andrew White, David A. Clifton, Marinka Zitnik

Biomedical knowledge graphs (KGs) are widely used in the life sciences, yet many are derived from unstructured documents and therefore lack schema-level constrains, whereas graphs assembled from structured resources are difficult to harmonize into a unified representation. We present OptimusKG, a multimodal biomedical labeled property graph (LPG) built from structured and semi-structured resources to preserve factual, type-specific metadata across molecular, anatomical, clinical, and environmental domains. OptimusKG contains 190,531 nodes across 10 entity types, 21,813,816 edges across 26 relation types, and 67,249,863 property instances encoding 110,276,843 values across 150 distinct property keys, derived from 18 ontologies and controlled vocabularies. The graph enforces a top-level schema for nodes and edges and retains granular, type-specific properties, cross-references, and provenance across molecular, anatomical, clinical, and environmental domains. We assessed the validity of OptimusKG by evaluating whether graph relationships are supported by evidence from the scientific literature using a multimodal agent, PaperQA3. PaperQA3 identified supporting evidence for 70.0% of sampled edges, whereas 83.4% of sampled false edges received no supporting evidence. Edges without literature support were concentrated in associations derived from experimental and functional genomics resources, suggesting that OptimusKG captures biomedical knowledge that may precede synthesis in the scientific literature. OptimusKG is distributed as Apache Parquet files, providing a standardized resource for graph-based machine learning, knowledge-grounded retrieval with large language models, and biomedical discovery use cases such as hypothesis generation.

摘要：生物醫學知識圖譜（KGs）在生命科學中被廣泛使用，但許多是從非結構化文件中衍生而來，因此缺乏模式層級的約束，而從結構化資源組成的圖則難以統一成一個統一的表示。<lb/>我們提出了OptimusKG，一個多模態生物醫學標記屬性圖（LPG），它是從結構化和半結構化資源中構建的，以保留分子、解剖、臨床和環境領域的事實性、類型特定的元數據。<lb/>OptimusKG包含190,531個節點，涵蓋10種實體類型，21,813,816條邊，涵蓋26種關係類型，以及67,249,863個屬性實例，編碼110,276,843個值，跨越150個不同的屬性鍵，這些數據源自18個本體和受控詞彙。<lb/>該圖對節點和邊施加了頂層模式，並保留了細粒度的、類型特定的屬性、交叉引用和來源，涵蓋分子、解剖、臨床和環境領域。<lb/>我們通過評估圖關係是否得到科學文獻的證據支持來評估OptimusKG的有效性，使用了一個多模態代理PaperQA3。<lb/>PaperQA3為70.0%的抽樣邊識別了支持證據，而83.4%的抽樣假邊則未獲得任何支持證據。<lb/>缺乏文獻支持的邊集中在從實驗和功能基因組資源衍生的關聯上，這表明OptimusKG捕捉了可能早於科學文獻中合成的生物醫學知識。<lb/>OptimusKG以Apache Parquet文件的形式分發，提供了一個標準化的資源，用於基於圖的機器學習、與大型語言模型的知識基礎檢索，以及生物醫學發現的用例，如假設生成。

##### **From Prompt to Physical Actuation: Holistic Threat Modeling of LLM-Enabled Robotic Systems**
2604.27267v1 by Neha Nagaraja, Hayretdin Bahsi, Carlo R. da Cunha

As large language models are integrated into autonomous robotic systems for task planning and control, compromised inputs or unsafe model outputs can propagate through the planning pipeline to physical-world consequences. Although prior work has studied robotic cybersecurity, adversarial perception attacks, and LLM safety independently, no existing study traces how these threat categories interact and propagate across trust boundaries in a unified architectural model. We address this gap by modeling an LLM-enabled autonomous robot in an edge-cloud architecture as a hierarchical Data Flow Diagram and applying STRIDE-per-interaction analysis across six boundary-crossing interaction points using a three-category taxonomy of Conventional Cyber Threats, Adversarial Threats, and Conversational Threats. The analysis reveals that these categories converge at the same boundary crossings, and we trace three cross-boundary attack chains from external entry points to unsafe physical actuation, each exposing a distinct architectural property: the absence of independent semantic validation between user input and actuator dispatch, cross-modal translation from visual perception to language-model instruction, and unmediated boundary crossing through provider-side tool use. To our knowledge, this is the first DFD-based threat analysis integrating all three threat categories across the full perception-planning-actuation pipeline of an LLM-enabled robotic system.

摘要：大型語言模型被整合進自主機器人系統中以進行任務規劃和控制，受損的輸入或不安全的模型輸出可能會通過規劃流程傳播到物理世界的後果。儘管先前的研究獨立探討了機器人網絡安全、對抗性感知攻擊和大型語言模型的安全性，但目前尚無研究追蹤這些威脅類別如何在統一的架構模型中互動並跨越信任邊界。我們通過將一個支持大型語言模型的自主機器人建模為邊緣-雲架構中的分層數據流圖，並在六個跨邊界的互動點上應用基於互動的STRIDE分析，來填補這一空白，使用傳統網絡威脅、對抗性威脅和對話威脅的三類分類法。分析顯示這些類別在相同的邊界交叉處匯聚，我們追蹤了三條跨邊界的攻擊鏈，從外部入口點到不安全的物理執行，每條鏈揭示了一個獨特的架構特性：用戶輸入與執行器調度之間缺乏獨立的語義驗證、從視覺感知到語言模型指令的跨模態翻譯，以及通過提供者端工具使用的無中介邊界跨越。據我們所知，這是首個基於數據流圖的威脅分析，整合了所有三類威脅，涵蓋了支持大型語言模型的機器人系統的完整感知-規劃-執行流程。

##### **Self-Evolving Software Agents**
2604.27264v1 by Marco Robol, Paolo Giorgini

Autonomous agents can adapt their behaviour to changing environments, but remain bound to requirements, goals, and capabilities fixed at design time, preventing genuine software evolution. This paper introduces self-evolving software agents, combining BDI reasoning with LLMs to enable autonomous evolution of goals, reasoning, and executable code. We propose a BDI-LLM architecture in which an automated evolution module operates alongside the agent's reasoning loop, eliciting new requirements from experience and synthesizing corresponding design and code updates. A prototype evaluated in a dynamic multi-agent environment shows that agents can autonomously discover new goals and generate executable behaviours from minimal prior knowledge. The results indicate both the feasibility and current limits of LLM-driven evolution, particularly in terms of behavioural inheritance and stability.

摘要：自主代理可以根據變化的環境調整其行為，但仍然受到設計時固定的需求、目標和能力的限制，這阻礙了真正的軟體演化。本文介紹了自我演化的軟體代理，結合BDI推理和LLM，使目標、推理和可執行代碼的自主演化成為可能。我們提出了一種BDI-LLM架構，其中自動演化模塊與代理的推理循環並行運作，從經驗中引出新需求並合成相應的設計和代碼更新。在一個動態多代理環境中評估的原型顯示，代理可以自主發現新目標並從最少的先驗知識中生成可執行行為。結果表明了LLM驅動演化的可行性及當前的限制，特別是在行為繼承和穩定性方面。

##### **AutoSurfer -- Teaching Web Agents through Comprehensive Surfing, Learning, and Modeling**
2604.27253v1 by Fazle Elahi Faisal, Qianhui Wu, Baolin Peng, Jianfeng Gao

Recent advances in multimodal large language models (LLMs) have revolutionized web agents that can automate complex tasks on websites. However, their accuracy remains limited by the scarcity of high-quality web trajectory training data. Existing automatic trajectory generation methods suffer from incomplete website coverage due to homepage-based task proposals or random-walk exploration. Such methods often result in hallucinated or ambiguous task synthesis that lead to incomplete and unreliable trajectory generation. Here, we present AutoSurfer, a comprehensive web trajectory generator that addresses these limitations through three key innovations. First, AutoSurfer employs a systematic breadth-first exploration strategy that maintains a queue of discovered pages and action traces, propagates knowledge across pages to avoid redundant exploration, and recursively expands multi-level graphical user interface elements - closely resembling how a human would learn a new website. Second, AutoSurfer leverages the exploration trajectory to guide task synthesis, reducing hallucinations by grounding complex tasks in actual navigation paths rather than isolated actions or page content alone. Third, AutoSurfer uses the same exploration trajectory as hints to steer a web agent toward more accurate and reliable trajectory refinement. Together, these innovations enable AutoSurfer to comprehensively cover a website's action space and generate data suitable for training website-specific LLMs. We evaluate AutoSurfer on the WebArena benchmark by fine-tuning Qwen2.5-VL-7B-Instruct and demonstrate that it outperforms state-of-the-art methods - Explorer, OS-Genesis, and SynthAgent - achieving up to 24.23% overall task completion accuracy compared to 19.59% for the best prior method. Further, task diversity analysis demonstrates that AutoSurfer yields a more diverse distribution of synthesized tasks.

摘要：最近在多模態大型語言模型（LLMs）方面的進展已經徹底改變了能夠自動化網站上複雜任務的網頁代理。然而，它們的準確性仍然受到高品質網頁軌跡訓練數據稀缺的限制。現有的自動軌跡生成方法因為基於首頁的任務提議或隨機漫遊探索而遭受網站覆蓋不完整的問題。這些方法通常會導致虛幻或模糊的任務合成，從而導致不完整和不可靠的軌跡生成。在此，我們提出了AutoSurfer，一個全面的網頁軌跡生成器，通過三個關鍵創新來解決這些限制。首先，AutoSurfer採用系統性的廣度優先探索策略，維護已發現頁面和行動痕跡的隊列，跨頁面傳播知識以避免冗餘探索，並遞歸擴展多層次的圖形用戶界面元素——這與人類學習新網站的方式非常相似。其次，AutoSurfer利用探索軌跡來指導任務合成，通過將複雜任務根植於實際導航路徑而不是孤立的行動或頁面內容，來減少幻覺的產生。第三，AutoSurfer使用相同的探索軌跡作為提示，引導網頁代理朝向更準確和可靠的軌跡精煉。這些創新使AutoSurfer能夠全面覆蓋網站的行動空間，並生成適合於訓練網站特定LLMs的數據。我們在WebArena基準上評估AutoSurfer，通過微調Qwen2.5-VL-7B-Instruct，並展示其超越最先進的方法——Explorer、OS-Genesis和SynthAgent，實現了高達24.23%的整體任務完成準確率，而最佳先前方法僅為19.59%。此外，任務多樣性分析顯示，AutoSurfer產生了更具多樣性的合成任務分佈。

##### **Reinforced Agent: Inference-Time Feedback for Tool-Calling Agents**
2604.27233v1 by Anh Ta, Junjie Zhu, Shahin Shayandeh

Tool-calling agents are evaluated on tool selection, parameter accuracy, and scope recognition, yet LLM trajectory assessments remain inherently post-hoc. Disconnected from the active execution loop, such assessments identify errors that are usually addressed through prompt-tuning or retraining, and fundamentally cannot course-correct the agent in real time. To close this gap, we move evaluation into the execution loop at inference time: a specialized reviewer agent evaluates provisional tool calls prior to execution, shifting the paradigm from post-hoc recovery to proactive evaluation and error mitigation.
  In practice, this architecture establishes a clear separation of concerns between the primary execution agent and a secondary review agent. As with any multi-agent system, the reviewer can introduce new errors while correcting others, yet no prior work to our knowledge has systematically measured this tradeoff. To quantify this tradeoff, we introduce Helpfulness-Harmfulness metrics: helpfulness measures the percentage of base agent errors that feedback corrects; harmfulness measures the percentage of correct responses that feedback degrades. These metrics directly inform reviewer design by revealing whether a given model or prompt provides net positive value.
  We evaluate our approach on BFCL (single-turn) and Tau2-Bench (multi-turn stateful scenarios), achieving +5.5% on irrelevance detection and +7.1% on multi-turn tasks. Our metrics reveal that reviewer model choice is critical: the reasoning model o3-mini achieves a 3:1 benefit-to-risk ratio versus 2.1:1 for GPT-4o. Automated prompt optimization via GEPA provides an additional +1.5-2.8%. Together, these results demonstrate a core advantage of separating execution and review: the reviewer can be systematically improved through model selection and prompt optimization, without retraining the base agent.

摘要：工具呼叫代理的評估基於工具選擇、參數準確性和範疇識別，但大型語言模型的軌跡評估本質上仍然是事後的。這些評估與主動執行循環脫節，識別出的錯誤通常通過提示調整或再訓練來解決，並且根本無法實時修正代理的行為。為了縮小這一差距，我們將評估移入推理時的執行循環：一個專門的審查代理在執行之前評估臨時的工具呼叫，將範式從事後恢復轉變為主動評估和錯誤減輕。<lb/>在實踐中，這種架構在主要執行代理和次要審查代理之間建立了明確的關注點分離。與任何多代理系統一樣，審查者在糾正其他錯誤的同時可能會引入新的錯誤，但據我們所知，之前的工作尚未系統性地測量這一權衡。為了量化這一權衡，我們引入了有用性-有害性指標：有用性衡量基礎代理錯誤中被反饋糾正的百分比；有害性衡量正確回應中被反饋降低的百分比。這些指標通過揭示給定模型或提示是否提供淨正價值，直接為審查者設計提供信息。<lb/>我們在BFCL（單回合）和Tau2-Bench（多回合有狀態場景）上評估我們的方法，實現了+5.5%的無關性檢測和+7.1%的多回合任務。我們的指標顯示，審查者模型的選擇至關重要：推理模型o3-mini達到了3:1的效益與風險比，而GPT-4o則為2.1:1。通過GEPA的自動提示優化提供了額外的+1.5-2.8%。綜合這些結果顯示了分離執行和審查的核心優勢：審查者可以通過模型選擇和提示優化系統性地改進，而無需重新訓練基礎代理。

##### **Upskilling with Generative AI: Practices and Challenges for Freelance Knowledge Workers**
2604.27231v1 by Kashif Imteyaz, Isabel Lopez, Nakul Rajpal, Hunjun Shin, Saiph Savage

Freelance workers must continually acquire new skills to remain competitive in online labor markets, yet they lack the organizational training, mentorship, and infrastructure available to traditional employees. Generative AI-powered tools like ChatGPT are reshaping market skill demands while also offering new forms of on-demand learning support to meet those demands. Despite growing interest in AI-powered learning tools, little is known about how freelancers actually use these tools to learn, the challenges they encounter, and how generative AI for learning interacts with precarity and competition in platform-based work. We present a mixed-methods study combining a survey and semi-structured interviews with freelance knowledge workers. Grounded in self-directed learning theory, we examine how freelancers integrate generative AI tools into their learning practices. Our findings show that freelancers increasingly rely on generative AI to structure learning and support exploratory skill acquisition, but do not treat it as their primary learning resource due to inconsistency, lack of contextual relevance, and verification overhead. We identify a shift from learning as growth to learning as survival, where upskilling is oriented toward immediate market viability rather than long-term development. We also surface a structural challenge we term invisible competencies, in which workers acquire skills through generative AI tools but lack credible ways to signal or validate these skills in competitive freelance markets. Based on these insights, we offer design recommendations for generative AI-powered learning tools for freelancers.

摘要：自由工作者必須不斷獲取新技能，以在在線勞動市場中保持競爭力，但他們缺乏傳統員工所擁有的組織培訓、導師指導和基礎設施。<lb/>像 ChatGPT 這樣的生成式 AI 工具正在重塑市場技能需求，同時也提供新的按需學習支持形式，以滿足這些需求。<lb/>儘管對 AI 驅動的學習工具的興趣日益增長，但對於自由工作者實際上如何使用這些工具進行學習、他們遇到的挑戰，以及生成式 AI 在學習中如何與平台工作中的不穩定性和競爭互動，仍知之甚少。<lb/>我們提出了一項混合方法研究，結合了對自由知識工作者的調查和半結構化訪談。<lb/>基於自我導向學習理論，我們考察了自由工作者如何將生成式 AI 工具整合到他們的學習實踐中。<lb/>我們的研究結果顯示，自由工作者越來越依賴生成式 AI 來結構化學習並支持探索性技能獲取，但由於不一致性、缺乏上下文相關性和驗證負擔，他們並不將其視為主要的學習資源。<lb/>我們發現了一種從成長學習轉變為生存學習的趨勢，其中技能提升的方向是針對即時市場可行性，而非長期發展。<lb/>我們還提出了一個結構性挑戰，稱之為隱形能力，工人通過生成式 AI 工具獲取技能，但在競爭激烈的自由市場中缺乏可信的方式來信號或驗證這些技能。<lb/>基於這些見解，我們為自由工作者的生成式 AI 驅動學習工具提供了設計建議。

##### **When Roles Fail: Epistemic Constraints on Advocate Role Fidelity in LLM-Based Political Statement Analysis**
2604.27228v1 by Juergen Dietrich

Democratic discourse analysis systems increasingly rely on multi-agent LLM pipelines in which distinct evaluator models are assigned adversarial roles to generate structured, multi-perspective assessments of political statements. A core assumption is that models will reliably maintain their assigned roles. This paper provides the first systematic empirical test of that assumption using the TRUST pipeline. We develop an epistemic stance classifier that identifies advocate roles from reasoning text without relying on surface vocabulary, and measure role fidelity across 60 political statements (30 English, 30 German) using four metrics: Role Drift Index (RDI), Expected Drift Distance (EDD), Directional Drift Index (DDI), and Entropy-based Role Stability (ERS). We identify two failure modes - the Epistemic Floor Effect (fact-check results create an absolute lower bound below which the legitimizing role cannot be maintained) and Role-Prior Conflict (training-time knowledge overrides role instructions for factually unambiguous statements) - as manifestations of a single mechanism: Epistemic Role Override (ERO). Model choice significantly affects role fidelity: Mistral Large outperforms Claude Sonnet by 28pp (67% vs. 39%) and exhibits a qualitatively different failure mode - role abandonment without polarity reversal - compared to Claude's active switch to the opposing stance. Role fidelity is language-robust. Fact-check provider choice is not universally neutral: Perplexity significantly reduces Claude's role fidelity on German statements (Delta = -15pp, p = 0.007) while leaving Mistral unaffected. These findings have direct implications for multi-agent LLM validation: a system validated without role fidelity measurement may systematically misrepresent the epistemic diversity it was designed to provide.

摘要：民主話語分析系統越來越依賴多代理 LLM 管道，其中不同的評估模型被分配對抗角色，以生成對政治聲明的結構化、多角度評估。核心假設是模型將可靠地維持其分配的角色。本文使用 TRUST 管道對該假設進行了首次系統的實證測試。我們開發了一個認識立場分類器，從推理文本中識別倡導者角色，而不依賴表面詞彙，並使用四個指標測量 60 條政治聲明（30 條英語，30 條德語）的角色忠誠度：角色漂移指數（RDI）、預期漂移距離（EDD）、方向性漂移指數（DDI）和基於熵的角色穩定性（ERS）。我們識別出兩種失敗模式 - 認識底效應（事實檢查結果創造了一個絕對下限，低於此下限的合法化角色無法維持）和角色優先衝突（訓練時的知識覆蓋了對事實明確聲明的角色指令） - 作為單一機制的表現：認識角色覆蓋（ERO）。模型選擇顯著影響角色忠誠度：Mistral Large 的表現超過 Claude Sonnet 28 個百分點（67% 對 39%），並顯示出質量上不同的失敗模式 - 角色放棄而不反轉極性 - 與 Claude 主動切換到對立立場相比。角色忠誠度在語言上是穩健的。事實檢查提供者的選擇並不普遍中立：Perplexity 顯著降低了 Claude 在德語聲明上的角色忠誠度（Delta = -15pp，p = 0.007），而對 Mistral 沒有影響。這些發現對多代理 LLM 驗證有直接的影響：未經角色忠誠度測量驗證的系統可能系統性地錯誤表示其設計提供的認識多樣性。

##### **TRUST: A Framework for Decentralized AI Service v.0.1**
2604.27132v1 by Yu-Chao Huang, Zhen Tan, Mohan Zhang, Pingzhi Li, Zhuo Zhang, Tianlong Chen

Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) and Multi-Agent Systems (MAS) in high-stakes domains demand reliable verification, yet centralized approaches suffer four limitations: (1) Robustness, with single points of failure vulnerable to attacks and bias; (2) Scalability, as reasoning complexity creates bottlenecks; (3) Opacity, as hidden auditing erodes trust; and (4) Privacy, as exposed reasoning traces risk model theft. We introduce TRUST (Transparent, Robust, and Unified Services for Trustworthy AI), a decentralized framework with three innovations: (i) Hierarchical Directed Acyclic Graphs (HDAGs) that decompose Chain-of-Thought reasoning into five abstraction levels for parallel distributed auditing; (ii) the DAAN protocol, which projects multi-agent interactions into Causal Interaction Graphs (CIGs) for deterministic root-cause attribution; and (iii) a multi-tier consensus mechanism among computational checkers, LLM evaluators, and human experts with stake-weighted voting that guarantees correctness under 30% adversarial participation. We prove a Safety-Profitability Theorem ensuring honest auditors profit while malicious actors incur losses. All decisions are recorded on-chain, while privacy-by-design segmentation prevents reconstruction of proprietary logic. Across multiple LLMs and benchmarks, TRUST attains 72.4% accuracy (4-18% above baselines) and remains resilient against 20% corruption. DAAN reaches 70% root-cause attribution (vs. 54-63% for standard methods) with 60% token savings. Human studies validate the design (F1 = 0.89, Brier = 0.074). The framework supports (A1) decentralized auditing, (A2) tamper-proof leaderboards, (A3) trustless data annotation, and (A4) governed autonomous agents, pioneering decentralized AI auditing for safe, accountable deployment of reasoning-capable systems.

摘要：大型推理模型（LRMs）和多代理系統（MAS）在高風險領域需要可靠的驗證，但集中式方法存在四個限制：（1）穩健性，單點故障容易受到攻擊和偏見的影響；（2）可擴展性，推理的複雜性造成瓶頸；（3）不透明性，隱藏的審計侵蝕信任；以及（4）隱私，暴露的推理痕跡存在模型被盜的風險。我們介紹了TRUST（透明、穩健和統一的可信AI服務），這是一個去中心化的框架，具有三項創新：（i）層次化有向無環圖（HDAGs），將思維鏈推理分解為五個抽象層次以進行平行分佈式審計；（ii）DAAN協議，將多代理互動投影到因果互動圖（CIGs）中，以進行確定性的根本原因歸因；以及（iii）在計算檢查者、LLM評估者和人類專家之間的多層共識機制，通過權重投票保證在30%對手參與下的正確性。我們證明了一個安全-獲利定理，確保誠實的審計者獲利，而惡意行為者則承受損失。所有決策都在鏈上記錄，而設計隱私分段防止重建專有邏輯。在多個LLM和基準測試中，TRUST達到了72.4%的準確率（比基準高出4-18%），並且在20%的腐敗情況下仍然保持穩健。DAAN達到70%的根本原因歸因（相比標準方法的54-63%），並節省了60%的令牌。人類研究驗證了設計（F1 = 0.89，Brier = 0.074）。該框架支持（A1）去中心化審計，（A2）防篡改的排行榜，（A3）無信任的數據標註，以及（A4）受管控的自主代理，開創了去中心化AI審計，為安全、負責任地部署具推理能力的系統奠定了基礎。

##### **Think it, Run it: Autonomous ML pipeline generation via self-healing multi-agent AI**
2604.27096v1 by Adela Bara, Gabriela Dobrita, Simona-Vasilica Oprea

The purpose of our paper is to develop a unified multi-agent architecture that automates end-to-end machine learning (ML) pipeline generation from datasets and natural-language (NL) goals, improving efficiency, robustness and explainability. A five-agent system is proposed to handle profiling, intent parsing, microservice recommendation, Directed Acyclic Graph (DAG) construction and execution. It integrates code-grounded Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) for microservice understanding, an explainable hybrid recommender combining multiple criteria, a self-healing mechanism using Large Language Model (LLM)-based error interpretation and adaptive learning from execution history. The approach is evaluated on 150 ML tasks across diverse scenarios. The system achieves an 84.7% end-to-end pipeline success rate, outperforming baseline methods. It demonstrates improved robustness through self-healing and reduces workflow development time compared to manual construction. The study introduces a novel integration of code-grounded RAG, explainable recommendation, self-healing execution and adaptive learning within a single architecture, showing that tightly coupled intelligent components can outperform isolated solutions.

摘要：我們的論文目的是開發一個統一的多代理架構，該架構自動化從數據集和自然語言（NL）目標生成端到端的機器學習（ML）管道，提高效率、穩健性和可解釋性。提出了一個五代理系統來處理配置檔、意圖解析、微服務推薦、有向無環圖（DAG）構建和執行。它整合了基於代碼的檢索增強生成（RAG）以理解微服務，結合多個標準的可解釋混合推薦系統，使用基於大型語言模型（LLM）的錯誤解釋和從執行歷史中自適應學習的自我修復機制。該方法在150個ML任務中進行評估，涵蓋多種情境。該系統實現了84.7%的端到端管道成功率，超越了基準方法。它通過自我修復顯示出改進的穩健性，並與手動構建相比減少了工作流程開發時間。這項研究在單一架構中引入了基於代碼的RAG、可解釋的推薦、自我修復執行和自適應學習的新整合，顯示出緊密耦合的智能組件可以超越孤立的解決方案。

##### **Useless but Safe? Benchmarking Utility Recovery with User Intent Clarification in Multi-Turn Conversations**
2604.27093v1 by Mingqian Zheng, Malia Morgan, Liwei Jiang, Carolyn Rose, Maarten Sap

Current LLM safety alignment techniques improve model robustness against adversarial attacks, but overlook whether and how LLMs can recover helpfulness when benign users clarify their intent. We introduce CarryOnBench, the first interactive benchmark that measures whether LLMs can revise their interpretation of user intent and recover utility, while remaining safe through multi-turn conversations. Starting from 398 seemingly harmful queries with benign underlying intents, we simulate 5,970 conversations by varying user follow-up sequences, evaluating 14 models on both intent-aligned utility and safety. CarryOnBench yields 1,866 different conversation flows of 4--12 turns, totaling 23,880 model responses. We design Ben-Util, a checklist-based metric that evaluates how well each model response fulfills the user's benign information need using atomic items. At turn one, models fulfill only 10.5--37.6% of the user's benign information need. When the same query includes the benign intent upfront, models fulfill 25.1--72.1%, confirming that models withhold information due to intent misinterpretation, not limited knowledge. With benign clarifications in multi-turn conversations, 13 of 14 models approach or exceed this single-turn baseline, yet recovery cost varies across models. We identify three failure modes invisible to single-turn evaluations: utility lock-in, where a model rarely updates despite clarification; unsafe recovery, where a model updates at disproportionate safety cost; and repetitive recovery, where a model recycles prior responses rather than providing new information. Moreover, conversations converge to similar harmfulness levels regardless of how conservative the model starts. These findings expose a gap that single-turn evaluations miss -- whether a model is appropriately cautious or simply unresponsive to clarified user intent.

摘要：目前的LLM安全對齊技術提高了模型對抗攻擊的魯棒性，但忽略了LLM在良性用戶澄清其意圖時，是否以及如何能夠恢復有用性。我們介紹了CarryOnBench，這是第一個互動基準，測量LLM是否能夠修正其對用戶意圖的解釋並恢復效用，同時在多輪對話中保持安全。從398個看似有害的查詢開始，這些查詢具有良性的潛在意圖，我們模擬了5,970次對話，通過變化用戶的後續序列，評估14個模型在意圖對齊效用和安全性方面的表現。CarryOnBench產生了1,866種不同的對話流程，包含4到12輪，共計23,880個模型回應。我們設計了Ben-Util，一種基於檢查表的指標，用於評估每個模型回應滿足用戶良性信息需求的程度，使用原子項目。在第一輪中，模型僅滿足用戶良性信息需求的10.5%至37.6%。當相同的查詢明確包含良性意圖時，模型滿足25.1%至72.1%，這證實了模型因意圖誤解而隱瞞信息，而不是知識有限。在多輪對話中進行良性澄清時，14個模型中的13個接近或超過這一單輪基準，但恢復成本在模型之間有所不同。我們識別了三種在單輪評估中不可見的失敗模式：效用鎖定，模型很少在澄清後更新；不安全的恢復，模型以不成比例的安全成本進行更新；以及重複恢復，模型重複之前的回應而不是提供新信息。此外，無論模型起始時多麼保守，對話都會收斂到相似的有害性水平。這些發現揭示了一個單輪評估所忽略的差距——模型是否適當謹慎，或僅僅對澄清的用戶意圖不作反應。

##### **End-to-end autonomous scientific discovery on a real optical platform**
2604.27092v1 by Shuxing Yang, Fujia Chen, Rui Zhao, Junyao Wu, Yize Wang, Haiyao Luo, Ning Han, Qiaolu Chen, Yuze Hu, Wenhao Li, Mingzhu Li, Hongsheng Chen, Yihao Yang

Scientific research has long been human-led, driving new knowledge and transformative technologies through the continual revision of questions, methods and claims as evidence accumulates. Although large language model (LLM)-based agents are beginning to move beyond assisting predefined research workflows, none has yet demonstrated end-to-end autonomous discovery in a real physical system that produces a nontrivial result supported by experimental evidence. Here we introduce Qiushi Discovery Engine, an LLM-based agentic system for end-to-end autonomous scientific discovery on a real optical platform. Qiushi Engine combines nonlinear research phases, Meta-Trace memory and a dual-layer architecture to maintain adaptive and stable research trajectories across long-horizon investigations involving thousands of LLM-mediated reasoning, measurement and revision actions. It autonomously reproduces a published transmission-matrix experiment on a non-original platform and converts an abstract coherence-order theory into experimental observables, providing, to our knowledge, the first observation of this class of coherence-order structure. More importantly, in an open-ended study involving 145.9 million tokens, 3,242 LLM calls, 1,242 tool calls, 163 research notes and 44 scripts, Qiushi Engine proposes and experimentally validates optical bilinear interaction, a physical mechanism structurally analogous to a core operation in Transformer attention. This AI-discovered mechanism suggests a route towards high-speed, energy-efficient optical hardware for pairwise computation. To our knowledge, this is the first demonstration of an AI agentic system autonomously identifying and experimentally validating a nontrivial, previously unreported physical mechanism, marking a milestone for research-level autonomous agents.

摘要：科學研究長期以來一直由人類主導，透過不斷修訂問題、方法和主張來推動新知識和變革性技術，隨著證據的積累而進行。儘管基於大型語言模型（LLM）的代理開始超越協助預定的研究工作流程，但尚未有任何代理在實際物理系統中展示出端到端的自主發現，並產生有實驗證據支持的非平凡結果。在此，我們介紹了 Qiushi Discovery Engine，一個基於 LLM 的自主科學發現系統，能在真實的光學平台上進行端到端的自主科學發現。Qiushi Engine 結合了非線性研究階段、Meta-Trace 記憶和雙層架構，以維持在涉及數千次 LLM 媒介推理、測量和修訂行動的長期調查中的適應性和穩定研究軌跡。它自主地重現了一個在非原始平台上的已發表傳輸矩陣實驗，並將一個抽象的相干序理論轉化為實驗可觀測量，據我們所知，這是首次觀察到這類相干序結構。更重要的是，在一項涉及 1.459 億個標記、3,242 次 LLM 調用、1,242 次工具調用、163 條研究筆記和 44 個腳本的開放式研究中，Qiushi Engine 提出了並實驗驗證了光學雙線性相互作用，這是一種在結構上類似於 Transformer 注意力中的核心操作的物理機制。這一 AI 發現的機制暗示了朝向高速度、節能的光學硬體進行成對計算的路徑。據我們所知，這是首次展示 AI 代理系統自主識別並實驗驗證一個非平凡的、先前未報告的物理機制，標誌著研究級自主代理的一個里程碑。

##### **Turning the TIDE: Cross-Architecture Distillation for Diffusion Large Language Models**
2604.26951v1 by Gongbo Zhang, Wen Wang, Ye Tian, Li Yuan

Diffusion large language models (dLLMs) offer parallel decoding and bidirectional context, but state-of-the-art dLLMs require billions of parameters for competitive performance. While existing distillation methods for dLLMs reduce inference steps within a single architecture, none address cross-architecture knowledge transfer, in which the teacher and student differ in architecture, attention mechanism, and tokenizer. We present TIDE, the first framework for cross-architecture dLLM distillation, comprising three modular components: (1) TIDAL, which jointly modulates distillation strength across training progress and diffusion timestep to account for the teacher's noise-dependent reliability; (2) CompDemo, which enriches the teacher's context via complementary mask splitting to improve predictions under heavy masking; and (3) Reverse CALM, a cross-tokenizer objective that inverts chunk-level likelihood matching, yielding bounded gradients and dual-end noise filtering. Distilling 8B dense and 16B MoE teachers into a 0.6B student via two heterogeneous pipelines outperforms the baseline by an average of 1.53 points across eight benchmarks, yielding notable gains in code generation, where HumanEval scores reach 48.78 compared to 32.3 for the AR baseline.

摘要：擴散大型語言模型（dLLMs）提供平行解碼和雙向上下文，但最先進的 dLLMs 需要數十億的參數以達到競爭性能。雖然現有的 dLLMs 蒸餾方法在單一架構內減少推理步驟，但沒有一種方法能解決跨架構知識轉移的問題，其中教師和學生在架構、注意力機制和標記器上有所不同。我們提出了 TIDE，第一個跨架構 dLLM 蒸餾框架，包含三個模組化組件：（1）TIDAL，該組件在訓練進展和擴散時間步驟中共同調節蒸餾強度，以考慮教師的噪聲依賴可靠性；（2）CompDemo，通過互補的掩碼分割來豐富教師的上下文，以改善在重度掩碼下的預測；以及（3）Reverse CALM，一個跨標記器的目標，反轉塊級似然匹配，產生有界梯度和雙端噪聲過濾。通過兩個異質管道將 8B 密集和 16B MoE 教師蒸餾為 0.6B 學生，在八個基準測試中平均超越基準 1.53 分，在代碼生成方面獲得顯著增益，其中 HumanEval 分數達到 48.78，相較於 AR 基準的 32.3。

##### **MoRFI: Monotonic Sparse Autoencoder Feature Identification**
2604.26866v1 by Dimitris Dimakopoulos, Shay B. Cohen, Ioannis Konstas

Large language models (LLMs) acquire most of their factual knowledge during the pre-training stage, through next token prediction. Subsequent stages of post-training often introduce new facts outwith the parametric knowledge, giving rise to hallucinations. While it has been demonstrated that supervised fine-tuning (SFT) on new knowledge may exacerbate the problem, the underlying mechanisms are still poorly understood. We conduct a controlled fine-tuning experiment, focusing on closed-book QA, and find latent directions that causally contribute to hallucinations. Specifically, we fine-tune Llama 3.1 8B, Gemma 2 9B and Mistral 7B v03 on seven distinct single QA datasets, controlling for the percentage of new knowledge and number of training epochs. By measuring performance on the test set, we validate that incrementally introducing new knowledge increases hallucinations, with the effect being more pronounced with prolonged training. We leverage pre-trained sparse autoencoders (SAEs) to analyze residual stream activations across various checkpoints for each model and propose Monotonic Relationship Feature Identification (MoRFI) for capturing causally relevant latents. MoRFI filters SAE features that respond monotonically to controlled fine-tuning data mixtures of a target property. Our findings show that exposure to unknown facts disrupts the model's ability to retrieve stored knowledge along a set of directions in the residual stream. Our pipeline reliably discovers them across distinct models, recovering knowledge through single-latent interventions.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在預訓練階段通過下一個標記預測獲得大部分事實知識。隨後的後訓練階段經常引入超出參數知識的新事實，導致幻覺的產生。雖然已經證明對新知識進行監督式微調（SFT）可能會加劇這個問題，但其潛在機制仍然不甚了解。我們進行了一項控制微調實驗，專注於閉卷問答，並發現潛在的方向會因果地促進幻覺的產生。具體來說，我們對 Llama 3.1 8B、Gemma 2 9B 和 Mistral 7B v03 在七個不同的單一問答數據集上進行微調，控制新知識的百分比和訓練週期的數量。通過測量測試集上的表現，我們驗證了逐步引入新知識會增加幻覺，且隨著訓練時間的延長，這一效應更加明顯。我們利用預訓練的稀疏自編碼器（SAEs）分析每個模型在各個檢查點的殘差流激活，並提出單調關係特徵識別（MoRFI）以捕捉因果相關的潛在變量。MoRFI 過濾對目標屬性的控制微調數據混合單調響應的 SAE 特徵。我們的研究結果顯示，接觸未知事實會干擾模型沿著一組方向檢索存儲知識的能力。我們的管道在不同模型中可靠地發現這些潛在變量，通過單一潛在干預恢復知識。

##### **Bian Que: An Agentic Framework with Flexible Skill Arrangement for Online System Operations**
2604.26805v1 by Bochao Liu, Zhipeng Qian, Yang Zhao, Xinyuan Jiang, Zihan Liang, Yufei Ma, Junpeng Zhuang, Ben Chen, Shuo Yang, Hongen Wan, Yao Wu, Chenyi Lei, Xiao Liang

Operating and maintaining (O&M) large-scale online engine systems (search, recommendation, advertising) demands substantial human effort for release monitoring, alert response, and root cause analysis. While LLM-based agents are a natural fit for these tasks, the deployment bottleneck is not reasoning capability but orchestration: selecting, for each operational event, the relevant data (metrics, logs, change events) and the applicable operational knowledge (handbook rules and practitioner experience). Feeding all signals indiscriminately causes dilution and hallucination, while manually curating the event-to-(data, knowledge) mapping is intractable under dozens of daily releases. We present Bian Que, an agentic framework with three contributions: (i) a \emph{unified operational paradigm} abstracting day-to-day O&M into three canonical patterns: release interception, proactive inspection, and alert root cause analysis; (ii) \emph{Flexible Skill Arrangement}, where each Skill specifies which data and knowledge to retrieve for a given business-module context and can be automatically generated and updated by LLMs or iteratively refined through natural-language instructions from on-call engineers; (iii) a \emph{unified self-evolving mechanism} in which one correction signal drives two parallel pathways, case-memory-to-knowledge distillation and targeted Skill refinement. Deployed on the e-commerce search engine of KuaiShou, the major short-video platform in China, Bian Que reduces alert volume by 75%, achieves 80% root-cause analysis accuracy, and cuts mean time to resolution by over 50%. Our framework achieves 99.0% pass rate on offline evaluations. Our code is available at https://github.com/benchen4395/BianQue_Assistant.

摘要：操作和維護（O&M）大規模在線引擎系統（搜索、推薦、廣告）需要大量的人力來進行版本監控、警報響應和根本原因分析。雖然基於LLM的代理非常適合這些任務，但部署瓶頸不在於推理能力，而在於協調：為每個操作事件選擇相關數據（指標、日誌、變更事件）和適用的操作知識（手冊規則和實踐經驗）。不加區別地提供所有信號會導致稀釋和幻覺，而手動策劃事件到（數據、知識）的映射在每日數十次的版本發布下是不可行的。我們提出了Bian Que，一個具有三個貢獻的代理框架：（i）一個\emph{統一操作範式}，將日常O&M抽象為三個典範模式：版本攔截、主動檢查和警報根本原因分析；（ii）\emph{靈活技能安排}，每個技能指定在給定業務模塊上下文中檢索哪些數據和知識，並可以由LLM自動生成和更新，或通過值班工程師的自然語言指令進行迭代精煉；（iii）一個\emph{統一自我演化機制}，其中一個修正信號驅動兩條平行路徑，即案例記憶到知識的蒸餾和針對性的技能精煉。部署在中國主要短視頻平台快手的電子商務搜索引擎上，Bian Que將警報量減少了75％，實現了80％的根本原因分析準確率，並將平均解決時間縮短了50％以上。我們的框架在離線評估中達到了99.0％的通過率。我們的代碼可在https://github.com/benchen4395/BianQue_Assistant獲得。

##### **NORACL: Neurogenesis for Oracle-free Resource-Adaptive Continual Learning**
2604.27031v1 by Karthik Charan Raghunathan, Christian Metzner, Laura Kriener, Melika Payvand

In a continual learning setting, we require a model to be plastic enough to learn a new task and stable enough to not disturb previously learned capabilities. We argue that this dilemma has an architectural root. A finite network has limited representational and plastic resources, yet the required capacity depends on properties of the future task stream that are unknown: how many tasks will be encountered, and how much they overlap in feature space. Regularization-based methods preserve past knowledge within fixed-capacity architectures and therefore implicitly rely on an oracle architecture sized for this unknown future. When tasks are only weakly related, fixed architectures progressively run out of plastic resources; when tasks are few or strongly overlapping, models are often over-provisioned. Inspired by neurogenesis in biology, we propose NORACL to address the stability-plasticity dilemma by tackling the oracle architecture problem through neuronal growth. Starting from a compact network, NORACL grows only when needed by monitoring two complementary signals for representational and plasticity saturation. We evaluate NORACL against oracle-sized static baselines across varying task counts and geometries. Across all settings, NORACL achieves final average accuracies that are better than or on par with oracle-provisioned static baselines while using fewer parameters. Additionally, NORACL yields architectures with interpretable growth, i.e. dissimilar tasks predominantly expand feature-extraction layers, whereas tasks which rely on common features shift growth toward later feature-combination layers. Our analysis further explains why fixed-capacity networks lose plasticity as tasks accumulate, whereas NORACL creates fresh capacity for new tasks through growth. Together, these results show that adaptive neurogenesis pushes the stability-plasticity Pareto frontier of continual learning.

摘要：在持續學習的環境中，我們需要一個模型，既要足夠靈活以學習新任務，又要足夠穩定以不干擾先前學習的能力。<lb/>我們認為這一困境有其架構上的根源。<lb/>有限的網絡擁有有限的表徵和可塑資源，而所需的容量取決於未來任務流的特性，這些特性是未知的：將會遇到多少任務，以及它們在特徵空間中的重疊程度。<lb/>基於正則化的方法在固定容量的架構中保留過去的知識，因此隱含地依賴於為這一未知未來設計的神諭架構。<lb/>當任務之間的關聯性較弱時，固定架構逐漸耗盡可塑資源；當任務較少或強烈重疊時，模型往往會過度配置。<lb/>受到生物學中神經生成的啟發，我們提出了NORACL，以通過神經元增長來解決穩定性-可塑性困境，並處理神諭架構問題。<lb/>從一個緊湊的網絡開始，NORACL僅在需要時增長，通過監控兩個互補信號來檢測表徵和可塑性飽和。<lb/>我們將NORACL與在不同任務數量和幾何形狀下的神諭大小靜態基準進行評估。<lb/>在所有設置中，NORACL達到了比神諭配置的靜態基準更好或相當的最終平均準確率，同時使用的參數更少。<lb/>此外，NORACL產生的架構具有可解釋的增長，即不相似的任務主要擴展特徵提取層，而依賴共同特徵的任務則將增長轉向後期特徵組合層。<lb/>我們的分析進一步解釋了為什麼固定容量的網絡在任務累積時會失去可塑性，而NORACL則通過增長為新任務創造新的容量。<lb/>綜合這些結果顯示，自適應神經生成推進了持續學習的穩定性-可塑性帕累托邊界。

##### **Decoupling Knowledge and Task Subspaces for Composable Parametric Retrieval Augmented Generation**
2604.26768v1 by Weihang Su, Hanwen Zhang, Qingyao Ai, Yiqun Liu

Parametric Retrieval-Augmented Generation (PRAG) encodes external documents into lightweight parameter modules that can be retrieved and merged at inference time, offering a promising alternative to in-context retrieval augmentation. Despite its potential, many PRAG implementations train document adapters with task-supervised objectives, which may cause each adapter to encode both document-specific facts and reusable task-solving behavior. This entanglement may make adapter composition less reliable: when multiple adapters are merged at inference time, their overlapping task behaviors can accumulate together with document-specific updates, potentially making the merged adapter less stable and less focused on the intended document knowledge. To examine this issue, we explore Orthogonal Subspace Decomposition (OSD), an adapter-training setup that separates reusable task behavior from document-specific knowledge adapters. Concretely, we first train a Task LoRA to capture reusable task behavior, and then train document LoRAs to encode document-specific knowledge in a orthogonal subspace. This setup provides a controlled way to examine how orthogonalizing task and document LoRA updates affects adapter composition in multi-document PRAG. Experiments across multiple knowledge-intensive tasks and model scales suggest that this orthogonalization strategy can improve compositional robustness in parametric RAG, especially when multiple document adapters are merged.

摘要：參數檢索增強生成（PRAG）將外部文檔編碼為輕量級參數模塊，這些模塊可以在推理時被檢索和合併，提供了一種有前景的替代方案來進行上下文檢索增強。儘管其潛力巨大，許多PRAG實現使用任務監督目標訓練文檔適配器，這可能導致每個適配器同時編碼文檔特定事實和可重用的任務解決行為。這種糾纏可能使得適配器的組合不那麼可靠：當多個適配器在推理時合併時，它們重疊的任務行為可能與文檔特定的更新一起累積，從而使合併的適配器不那麼穩定，且不那麼專注於預期的文檔知識。為了檢查這個問題，我們探索了正交子空間分解（OSD），這是一種將可重用的任務行為與文檔特定知識適配器分開的適配器訓練設置。具體來說，我們首先訓練一個任務LoRA來捕捉可重用的任務行為，然後訓練文檔LoRA來在正交子空間中編碼文檔特定知識。這種設置提供了一種受控的方法來檢查正交化任務和文檔LoRA更新如何影響多文檔PRAG中的適配器組合。在多個知識密集型任務和模型規模上的實驗表明，這種正交化策略可以改善參數RAG中的組合穩健性，特別是在合併多個文檔適配器時。

##### **Exploring the Potential of Probabilistic Transformer for Time Series Modeling: A Report on the ST-PT Framework**
2604.26762v1 by Zhangzhi Xiong, Haoyi Wu, You Wu, Shuqi Gu, Kan Ren, Kewei Tu

The Probabilistic Transformer (PT) establishes that the Transformer's self-attention plus its feed-forward block is mathematically equivalent to Mean-Field Variational Inference (MFVI) on a Conditional Random Field (CRF). Under this equivalence the Transformer ceases to be a black-box neural network and becomes a programmable factor graph: graph topology, factor potentials, and the message-passing schedule are all explicit and inspectable primitives that can be engineered. PT was originally developed for natural language and in this report we investigate its potential for time series. We first lift PT into the Spatial-Temporal Probabilistic Transformer (ST-PT) to repair PT's missing channel axis and weak per-step semantics, and adopt ST-PT as a shared cornerstone backbone. We then identify three distinct properties that PT/ST-PT offers as a factor-graph model and derive three Research Questions, one per property, that probe how each property can be exploited in time series: RQ1. The graph topology and potentials are direct programmable primitives. Can this be used to inject symbolic time-series priors into ST-PT through structural graph modifications, especially under data scarcity and noise? RQ2. The CRF's factor matrices are the operator's potentials. Can an external condition program these factor matrices on a per-sample basis, so that conditional generation becomes structural rather than feature-level modulation of a fixed one? RQ3. Each MFVI iteration is a Bayesian posterior update on the factor graph. Can this turn the latent transition of latent-space AutoRegressive (AR) forecasting from an opaque MLP into a principled posterior update, and can a CRF teacher distill its latents into the AR student to counter cumulative error? We give one empirical study per question. Together, these three studies position ST-PT as a programmable framework for time-series modeling.

摘要：概率Transformer（PT）確立了Transformer的自注意力加上其前饋區塊在數學上等同於條件隨機場（CRF）上的均場變分推斷（MFVI）。在這種等價性下，Transformer不再是一個黑箱神經網絡，而是成為一個可編程的因子圖：圖的拓撲、因子潛能和消息傳遞計劃都是明確且可檢查的原始元件，可以進行工程設計。PT 最初是為自然語言開發的，在本報告中，我們探討其在時間序列中的潛力。我們首先將 PT 提升為空間-時間概率Transformer（ST-PT），以修復 PT 缺失的通道軸和弱每步語義，並將 ST-PT 作為共享的基石骨幹。我們然後確定了 PT/ST-PT 作為因子圖模型所提供的三個不同特性，並推導出三個研究問題，每個特性一個，探討如何在時間序列中利用每個特性：RQ1。圖的拓撲和潛能是直接可編程的原始元件。這是否可以用來通過結構圖修改將符號時間序列先驗注入 ST-PT，特別是在數據稀缺和噪聲的情況下？RQ2。CRF 的因子矩陣是運算子的潛能。外部條件能否在每個樣本的基礎上編程這些因子矩陣，使得條件生成成為結構性而非固定一個的特徵級調制？RQ3。每次 MFVI 迭代都是因子圖上的貝葉斯後驗更新。這是否能將潛在空間自回歸（AR）預測的潛在轉換從不透明的 MLP 轉變為有原則的後驗更新，並且 CRF 教師能否將其潛在轉化為 AR 學生以抵消累積誤差？我們針對每個問題提供一項實證研究。這三項研究共同將 ST-PT 定位為一個可編程的時間序列建模框架。

##### **Atomic-Probe Governance for Skill Updates in Compositional Robot Policies**
2604.26689v1 by Xue Qin, Simin Luan, John See, Cong Yang, Zhijun Li

Skill libraries in deployed robotic systems are continually updated through fine-tuning, fresh demonstrations, or domain adaptation, yet existing typed-composition methods (BLADE, SymSkill, Generative Skill Chaining) treat the library as frozen at test time and do not analyze how composition outcomes change when a skill is replaced. We introduce a paired-sampling cross-version swap protocol on robosuite manipulation tasks to characterize this dimension of compositional skill learning. On a dual-arm peg-in-hole task we discover a dominant-skill effect: one ECM achieves 86.7% atomic success rate while every other ECM is at or below 26.7%, and whether this dominant ECM enters a composition shifts the success rate by up to +50pp. We characterize the boundary on a simpler pick task where all atomic policies saturate at 100% and the effect is undefined. Across three tasks we further find that off-policy behavioral distance metrics fail to identify the dominant ECM, ruling out the natural cheap predictor. We propose an atomic-quality probe and a Hybrid Selector combining per-skill probes (zero per-decision cost) with selective composition revalidation (full cost), and characterize its Pareto frontier on 144 skill-update decisions. On T6 the atomic-only probe sits 23pp below full revalidation (64.6% vs 87.5% oracle match) at zero per-decision cost; a Hybrid Selector with m=10 closes most of that gap to ~12pp at 46% of full-revalidation cost. On the cross-task average over 144 events, atomic-only is within 3pp of full revalidation under a mixed-oracle caveat. The atomic-quality probe is, to our knowledge, the first principled, deployment-ready primitive for skill-update governance in compositional robot policies.

摘要：已部署的機器人系統中的技能庫通過微調、新的示範或領域適應不斷更新，然而現有的類型組合方法（BLADE、SymSkill、Generative Skill Chaining）在測試時將庫視為凍結，並未分析當技能被替換時組合結果如何變化。我們在robosuite操作任務上引入了一種配對抽樣的跨版本交換協議，以表徵這一組合技能學習的維度。在一個雙臂插釘任務中，我們發現了一種主導技能效應：一個ECM達到了86.7%的原子成功率，而其他每個ECM的成功率均在或低於26.7%，並且這個主導ECM是否進入組合會使成功率變化高達+50pp。我們在一個更簡單的拾取任務中表徵了邊界，所有原子策略的成功率飽和在100%，而效果則未定義。在三個任務中，我們進一步發現，離線策略行為距離度量無法識別主導ECM，排除了自然的廉價預測器。我們提出了一種原子質量探測器和一種混合選擇器，將每個技能的探測器（每次決策成本為零）與選擇性組合重新驗證（全成本）結合起來，並在144次技能更新決策上表徵其帕累托邊界。在T6中，僅原子探測器的表現比完全重新驗證低23pp（64.6%對87.5%預測匹配），且每次決策成本為零；一個m=10的混合選擇器將這一差距縮小到約12pp，成本為完全重新驗證的46%。在144次事件的跨任務平均中，僅原子探測器在混合預測的警告下與完全重新驗證相差不超過3pp。據我們所知，原子質量探測器是第一個原則性、準備部署的原始工具，用於組合機器人政策中的技能更新治理。

##### **When to Retrieve During Reasoning: Adaptive Retrieval for Large Reasoning Models**
2604.26649v1 by Dongxin Guo, Jikun Wu, Siu Ming Yiu

Large reasoning models such as DeepSeek-R1 and OpenAI o1 generate extended chains of thought spanning thousands of tokens, yet their integration with retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) remains fundamentally misaligned. Current RAG systems optimize for providing context before reasoning begins, while reasoning models require evidence injection during multi-step inference chains. We introduce ReaLM-Retrieve, a reasoning-aware retrieval framework that addresses this mismatch through three key innovations: (1) a step-level uncertainty detector that identifies knowledge gaps at reasoning-step granularity rather than token or sentence level; (2) a retrieval intervention policy that learns when external evidence maximally benefits ongoing reasoning; and (3) an efficiency-optimized integration mechanism that reduces per-retrieval overhead by 3.2x compared to naive integration. Experiments on MuSiQue, HotpotQA, and 2WikiMultiHopQA demonstrate that ReaLM-Retrieve achieves on average 10.1% absolute improvement in answer F1 over standard RAG (range: 9.0-11.8% across the three benchmarks) while reducing retrieval calls by 47% compared to fixed-interval approaches like IRCoT (all improvements significant at p<0.01, paired bootstrap). On the challenging MuSiQue benchmark requiring 2-4 hop reasoning, our method achieves 71.2% F1 with an average of only 1.8 retrieval calls per question. Analysis shows that ReaLM-Retrieve also improves retrieval quality itself, achieving 81.3% Recall@5 with consistently higher precision and MRR than fixed-interval baselines on supporting evidence, establishing new state-of-the-art efficiency-accuracy trade-offs for reasoning-intensive retrieval tasks.

摘要：大型推理模型如 DeepSeek-R1 和 OpenAI o1 生成延伸的思考鏈，跨越數千個標記，但它們與檢索增強生成（RAG）的整合仍然根本不對齊。當前的 RAG 系統優化於在推理開始之前提供上下文，而推理模型則需要在多步推理鏈中進行證據注入。我們介紹了 ReaLM-Retrieve，一個考慮推理的檢索框架，通過三個關鍵創新來解決這一不匹配問題：（1）一個步驟級的不確定性檢測器，能夠在推理步驟的粒度上識別知識缺口，而不是在標記或句子級別；（2）一個檢索干預政策，學習何時外部證據對正在進行的推理帶來最大益處；（3）一個效率優化的整合機制，與天真的整合相比，每次檢索的開銷減少了 3.2 倍。對 MuSiQue、HotpotQA 和 2WikiMultiHopQA 的實驗顯示，ReaLM-Retrieve 在答案 F1 上平均實現了 10.1% 的絕對提升，相對於標準 RAG（在三個基準上範圍：9.0-11.8%），同時與固定間隔方法如 IRCoT 相比，檢索調用減少了 47%（所有改進在 p&lt;0.01 的配對自助法下顯著）。在需要 2-4 步推理的挑戰性 MuSiQue 基準上，我們的方法實現了 71.2% 的 F1，每個問題平均僅需 1.8 次檢索調用。分析顯示，ReaLM-Retrieve 還改善了檢索質量，實現了 81.3% 的 Recall@5，並在支持證據上始終保持比固定間隔基準更高的精確度和 MRR，為推理密集型檢索任務建立了新的最先進效率-準確性權衡。

##### **SciHorizon-DataEVA: An Agentic System for AI-Readiness Evaluation of Heterogeneous Scientific Data**
2604.26645v1 by Dianyu Liu, Chuan Qin, Xi Chen, Xiaohan Li, Wenxi Xu, Yuyang Wang, Xin Chen, Yuanchun Zhou, Hengshu Zhu

AI-for-Science (AI4Science) is increasingly transforming scientific discovery by embedding machine learning models into prediction, simulation, and hypothesis generation workflows across domains. However, the effectiveness of these models is fundamentally constrained by the AI-readiness of scientific data, for which no scalable and systematic evaluation mechanism currently exists. In this work, we propose SciHorizon-DataEVA, a novel agentic system to scalable AI-readiness evaluation of heterogeneous scientific data. At the evaluation-criteria level, we introduce the Sci-TQA2 principles, which organize AI-readiness into four complementary dimensions: Governance Trustworthiness, Data Quality, AI Compatibility, and Scientific Adaptability. Each dimension is decomposed into measurable atomic elements that enable fine-grained and executable assessment. To operationalize these principles at scale, we develop Sci-TQA2-Eval, a hierarchical multi-agent evaluation approach orchestrated through a directed, cyclic workflow. Our Sci-TQA2-Eval dynamically constructs dataset-aware evaluation specifications by combining lightweight dataset profiling, applicability-aware metric activation, and knowledge-augmented planning grounded in domain constraints and dataset-paper signals. These specifications are executed through an adaptive, tool-centric evaluation mechanism with built-in verification and self-correction, enabling scalable and reliable assessment across heterogeneous scientific data. Extensive experiments on scientific datasets spanning multiple domains demonstrate the effectiveness and generality of SciHorizon-DataEVA for principled AI-readiness evaluation.

摘要：AI-for-Science (AI4Science) 正在透過將機器學習模型嵌入預測、模擬和假設生成工作流程中，越來越多地改變科學發現。<lb/>然而，這些模型的有效性根本上受到科學數據的 AI 準備程度的限制，目前尚不存在可擴展和系統化的評估機制。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們提出了 SciHorizon-DataEVA，一個新穎的代理系統，用於異質科學數據的可擴展 AI 準備評估。<lb/>在評估標準層面上，我們引入了 Sci-TQA2 原則，將 AI 準備劃分為四個互補的維度：治理可信度、數據質量、AI 兼容性和科學適應性。<lb/>每個維度被分解為可測量的原子元素，從而實現細緻且可執行的評估。<lb/>為了在規模上實現這些原則，我們開發了 Sci-TQA2-Eval，一種通過有向循環工作流程協調的分層多代理評估方法。<lb/>我們的 Sci-TQA2-Eval 通過結合輕量級數據集剖析、適用性感知的度量激活和基於領域約束及數據集-論文信號的知識增強規劃，動態構建數據集感知的評估規範。<lb/>這些規範通過具有內建驗證和自我修正的自適應工具中心評估機制執行，使得在異質科學數據上能夠進行可擴展和可靠的評估。<lb/>在跨多個領域的科學數據集上進行的廣泛實驗展示了 SciHorizon-DataEVA 在原則性 AI 準備評估中的有效性和普遍性。

##### **SAGE: A Strategy-Aware Graph-Enhanced Generation Framework For Online Counseling**
2604.26630v1 by Eliya Naomi Aharon, Meytal Grimland, Avi Segal, Loona Ben Dayan, Inbar Shenfeld, Yossi Levi Belz, Kobi Gal

Effective mental health counseling is a complex, theory-driven process requiring the simultaneous integration of psychological frameworks, real-time distress signals, and strategic intervention planning. This level of clinical reasoning is critical for safety and therapeutic effectiveness but is often missing in general-purpose Large Language Models (LLMs). We introduce SAGE (Strategy-Aware Graph-Enhanced), a novel framework designed to bridge the gap between structured clinical knowledge and generative AI. SAGE constructs a heterogeneous graph that unifies conversational dynamics with a psychologically grounded layer, explicitly anchoring interactions in a theory-driven lexicon. Our architecture first employs a Next Strategy Classifier to identify the optimal therapeutic intervention. Subsequently, a Graph-Aware Attention mechanism projects graph-derived structural signals into soft prompts, conditioning the LLM to generate responses that maintain clinical depth. Validated through both automated metrics and expert human evaluation, SAGE outperforms baselines in strategy prediction and recommended response quality. By providing actionable intervention recommendations, SAGE serves as a cutting-edge decision-support tool designed to augment human expertise in high-stakes crisis counseling.

摘要：有效的心理健康諮詢是一個複雜的、以理論為驅動的過程，需要同時整合心理框架、即時的痛苦信號和戰略干預計劃。這種臨床推理的水平對於安全性和治療效果至關重要，但在通用的大型語言模型（LLMs）中往往缺失。我們介紹了SAGE（策略感知圖增強），這是一個旨在彌合結構化臨床知識與生成式人工智慧之間差距的新框架。SAGE構建了一個異質圖，將對話動態與心理學基礎層統一，明確地將互動錨定在以理論為驅動的詞彙中。我們的架構首先使用下一步策略分類器來識別最佳的治療干預。隨後，圖感知注意力機制將圖派生的結構信號投影到柔性提示中，調整LLM以生成保持臨床深度的回應。通過自動化指標和專家人員評估的驗證，SAGE在策略預測和建議回應質量方面超越了基準。通過提供可行的干預建議，SAGE作為一個尖端的決策支持工具，旨在增強人類在高風險危機諮詢中的專業知識。

##### **Human-in-the-Loop Benchmarking of Heterogeneous LLMs for Automated Competency Assessment in Secondary Level Mathematics**
2604.26607v1 by Jatin Bhusal, Nancy Mahatha, Aayush Acharya, Raunak Regmi

As Competency-Based Education (CBE) is gaining traction around the world, the shift from marks-based assessment to qualitative competency mapping is a manual challenge for educators. This paper tackles the bottleneck issue by suggesting a "Human-in-the-Loop" benchmarking framework to assess the effectiveness of multiple LLMs in automating secondary-level mathematics assessment. Based on the Grade 10 Optional Mathematics curriculum in Nepal, we created a multi-dimensional rubric for four topics and four cross-cutting competencies: Comprehension, Knowledge, Operational Fluency, and Behavior and Correlation.
  The multi-provider ensemble, consisted of open-weight models -- Eagle (Llama 3.1-8B) and Orion (Llama 3.3-70B) -- and proprietary frontier models Nova (Gemini 2.5 Flash) and Lyra (Gemini 3 Pro), was benchmarked against a ground truth defined by two senior mathematics faculty members (kappa_w = 0.8652). The findings show a marked "Architecture-compatibility gap". Although the Gemini-based Mixture-of-Experts (Sparse MoE) models achieved "Fair Agreement" (kappa_w ~ 0.38), the larger Orion (70B) model exhibited "No Agreement" (kappa_w = -0.0261), suggesting that architectural compliance with instruction constraints outweighs the scale of raw parameters in rubric-constrained tasks. We conclude that while LLMs are not yet suitable for autonomous certification, they provide high-value assistive support for preliminary evidence extraction within a "Human-in-the-Loop" framework.

摘要：隨著以能力為基礎的教育（CBE）在全球獲得關注，從基於分數的評估轉向質性能力映射對教育工作者來說是一項手動挑戰。本文通過提出一個“人類參與”的基準框架來解決瓶頸問題，以評估多個大型語言模型（LLMs）在自動化中學數學評估中的有效性。基於尼泊爾的十年級選修數學課程，我們為四個主題和四個跨領域能力創建了一個多維度評分標準：理解、知識、操作流暢性以及行為和相關性。<lb/>由開放權重模型——Eagle（Llama 3.1-8B）和Orion（Llama 3.3-70B）以及專有前沿模型Nova（Gemini 2.5 Flash）和Lyra（Gemini 3 Pro）組成的多提供者集成，與由兩位資深數學教師定義的真實基準進行了基準測試（kappa_w = 0.8652）。研究結果顯示出明顯的“架構相容性差距”。雖然基於Gemini的專家混合模型（Sparse MoE）達到了“公平協議”（kappa_w ~ 0.38），但更大的Orion（70B）模型顯示出“無協議”（kappa_w = -0.0261），這表明在受評分標準約束的任務中，架構遵循教學約束的合規性超過了原始參數的規模。我們得出結論，儘管LLMs尚不適合自動認證，但它們在“人類參與”框架內提供了高價值的輔助支持，用於初步證據提取。

##### **Graph Construction and Matching for Imperative Programs using Neural and Structural Methods**
2604.26578v1 by Arshad Beg, Diarmuid O'Donoghue, Rosemary Monahan

Reusing verification artefacts requires identifying structural and semantic similarities across programs and their specifications. In this paper, we focus on graph construction as a foundational step toward this goal. We present a pipeline that converts imperative programs and their annotations into typed, attributed graphs. ##### **AGEL-Comp: A Neuro-Symbolic Framework for Compositional Generalization in Interactive Agents**
2604.26522v1 by Mahnoor Shahid, Hannes Rothe

Large Language Model (LLM)-based agents exhibit systemic failures in compositional generalization, limiting their robustness in interactive environments. This work introduces AGEL-Comp, a neuro-symbolic AI agent architecture designed to address this challenge by grounding actions of the agent. AGEL-Comp integrates three core innovations: (1) a dynamic Causal Program Graph (CPG) as a world model, representing procedural and causal knowledge as a directed hypergraph; (2) an Inductive Logic Programming (ILP) engine that synthesizes new Horn clauses from experiential feedback, grounding symbolic knowledge through interaction; and (3) a hybrid reasoning core where an LLM proposes a set of candidate sub-goals that are verified for logical consistency by a Neural Theorem Prover (NTP). Together, these components operationalize a deduction--abduction learning cycle: enabling the agent to deduce plans and abductively expand its symbolic world model, while a neural adaptation phase keeps its reasoning engine aligned with new knowledge. We propose an evaluation protocol within the \texttt{Retro Quest} simulation environment to probe for compositional generalization scenarios to evaluate our AGEL agent. Our findings clearly indicate the better performance of our AGEL model over pure LLM-based models. Our framework presents a principled path toward agents that build an explicit, interpretable, and compositionally structured understanding of their world.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLM）基礎的代理在組合泛化方面表現出系統性失敗，限制了它們在互動環境中的穩健性。這項工作介紹了 AGEL-Comp，一種神經符號 AI 代理架構，旨在通過將代理的行動具體化來應對這一挑戰。AGEL-Comp 整合了三項核心創新：（1）一個動態因果程序圖（CPG）作為世界模型，將程序性和因果知識表示為有向超圖；（2）一個歸納邏輯編程（ILP）引擎，從經驗反饋中合成新的霍恩子句，通過互動將符號知識具體化；以及（3）一個混合推理核心，其中 LLM 提出一組候選子目標，這些目標由神經定理證明器（NTP）驗證邏輯一致性。這些組件共同實現了一個推理--歸納學習循環：使代理能夠推導計劃並歸納性地擴展其符號世界模型，同時神經適應階段保持其推理引擎與新知識的一致性。我們在 \texttt{Retro Quest} 模擬環境中提出了一個評估協議，以探測組合泛化場景來評估我們的 AGEL 代理。我們的研究結果明確表明，我們的 AGEL 模型在性能上優於純 LLM 基礎模型。我們的框架為構建對其世界有明確、可解釋和組合結構理解的代理提供了一條原則性途徑。

##### **Auto-Relational Reasoning**

##### **QYOLO: Lightweight Object Detection via Quantum Inspired Shared Channel Mixing**
2604.26435v1 by Garvit Kumar Mittal, Sahil Tomar, Sandeep Kumar

The rapid advancement of object detection architectures has positioned single stage detectors as the dominant solution for real-time visual perception. A primary source of computational overhead in these models lies in the deep backbone stages, where C2f bottleneck modules at high stride levels accumulate a disproportionate share of parameters due to quadratic scaling with channel width. This work introduces QYOLO, a quantum-inspired channel mixing framework that achieves genuine architectural compression by replacing the two deepest backbone C2f modules at P4/16 (512 channels) and P5/32 (1024 channels) with a compact QMixBlock. The proposed block performs global channel recalibration through a sinusoidal mixing mechanism with shared learnable parameters across both backbone stages, enforcing consistent channel importance without requiring independent per-stage parameter sets. The neck and detection head remain fully classical and unchanged. Evaluation on the VisDrone2019 benchmark demonstrates that QYOLOv8n achieves a 20.2% reduction in parameter count (3.01M to 2.40M) and 12.3% GFLOPs reduction with only 0.4 pp mAP@50 degradation. QYOLOv8s achieves 21.8% reduction with 0.1 pp degradation. When combined with knowledge distillation, full accuracy parity is recovered at no cost to compression. An expanded backbone plus neck variant achieved 38 to 41% reduction at the cost of greater accuracy degradation, motivating the backbone-only final design.

摘要：單階檢測器的快速進展使其成為實時視覺感知的主導解決方案。這些模型中的主要計算開銷來源於深層主幹階段，其中高步幅水平的C2f瓶頸模塊由於通道寬度的二次擴展而累積了不成比例的參數份額。本研究介紹了QYOLO，一種量子啟發的通道混合框架，通過用緊湊的QMixBlock替換P4/16（512通道）和P5/32（1024通道）中最深的兩個主幹C2f模塊來實現真正的架構壓縮。所提出的模塊通過一種正弦混合機制執行全局通道重新校準，並在兩個主幹階段之間共享可學習的參數，強制實現一致的通道重要性，而無需獨立的每階段參數集。頸部和檢測頭保持完全經典且不變。在VisDrone2019基準上的評估表明，QYOLOv8n實現了20.2%的參數數量減少（從3.01M減少到2.40M）和12.3%的GFLOPs減少，僅有0.4 pp的mAP@50降級。QYOLOv8s實現了21.8%的減少，降級為0.1 pp。當與知識蒸餾結合時，完全的準確性平衡在不影響壓縮的情況下得以恢復。一個擴展的主幹加頸部變體在更大的準確性降級成本下實現了38%至41%的減少，這促使了僅主幹的最終設計。

##### **STLGT: A Scalable Trace-Based Linear Graph Transformer for Tail Latency Prediction in Microservices**
2604.26422v1 by Yongliang Ding, Qigong Bi, Peng Pu

Accurate end-to-end tail-latency forecasting is critical for proactive SLO management in microservice systems. However, modeling long-range dependency propagation and non-stationary, bursty workloads while maintaining inference efficiency at scale remains challenging. We present STLGT (Scalable Trace-based Linear Graph Transformer), a per-API predictor that encodes traces as span graphs for multi-step p95 tail-latency forecasting. STLGT uses a structure-aware linear graph Transformer to propagate cross-service dependencies with inference time linear in span graph size, and a decoupled temporal module to capture workload dynamics. Across a personalized education microservice application, DeathStarBench, and Alibaba traces, STLGT improves forecasting accuracy over PERT-GNN by 8.5% MAPE on average and achieves up to 12x faster CPU inference at N=32, matching the maximum span graph size after preprocessing the Alibaba traces. ##### **Delineating Knowledge Boundaries for Honest Large Vision-Language Models**
2604.26419v1 by Junru Song, Yimeng Hu, Yijing Chen, Huining Li, Qian Li, Lizhen Cui, Yuntao Du

Large Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have achieved remarkable multimodal performance yet remain prone to factual hallucinations, particularly in long-tail or specialized domains. Moreover, current models exhibit a weak capacity to refuse queries that exceed their parametric knowledge. In this paper, we propose a systematic framework to enhance the refusal capability of VLMs when facing such unknown questions. We first curate a model-specific "Visual-Idk" (Visual-I don't know) dataset, leveraging multi-sample consistency probing to distinguish between known and unknown facts. We then align the model using supervised fine-tuning followed by preference-aware optimization (e.g., DPO, ORPO) to effectively delineate its knowledge boundaries. Results on the Visual-Idk dataset show our method improves the Truthful Rate from 57.9\% to 67.3\%. Additionally, internal probing also demonstrates that the model genuinely recognizes its boundaries instead of just memorizing refusal patterns. Our framework further generalizes to out-of-distribution medical and perceptual domains, providing a robust path toward more trustworthy and prudent visual assistants.
